-----title
新绛（正平）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d6b56e0c7caf4604ba48e6f1596b236b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d6b56e0c7caf4604ba48e6f1596b236b");'><span id='d6b56e0c7caf4604ba48e6f1596b236b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=779')">777-779年</a>，12-14岁</div><div id='d6b56e0c7caf4604ba48e6f1596b236b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　本年前后，父官正平尉。楚当随父赴任，因识李景略，并为李所见重。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=778&endYear=779')">778-779年</a>　本年前后，父官正平尉。楚当随父赴任。<br /></div>

-----title
西安（长安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='99dc48e01e654bf192a7f3ec09da33e2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("99dc48e01e654bf192a7f3ec09da33e2");'><span id='99dc48e01e654bf192a7f3ec09da33e2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=789')">785-789年</a>，20-24岁</div><div id='99dc48e01e654bf192a7f3ec09da33e2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=789')">785-789年</a>　曾应试落第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e5b9b77eb8244ddc8a9b930eea99d168_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e5b9b77eb8244ddc8a9b930eea99d168");'><span id='e5b9b77eb8244ddc8a9b930eea99d168_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=791&endYear=791')">791年</a>，26岁</div><div id='e5b9b77eb8244ddc8a9b930eea99d168' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>本年令狐楚为同榜状元尹枢荐引，以第五名进士第。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>省试《珠还合浦赋》、《青云干吕》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span>《青云干吕》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_1370305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>珠还合浦赋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（791年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370305")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370305_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1370305_0'>① 以不贪为宝神物自还为韵　一作还珠亭赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370305'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370305'>物之多兮珠为珍。通其货而济乎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370305_comment'></div>才披沙以皛耀。俄错彩以璘玢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370305_comment'></div>避无厌之心。去之他境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370305_comment'></div>归克俭之政。还乎旧津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370305_comment'></div>由是观德。孰云无神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370305_comment'></div>相彼南州。昔无廉吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370305_comment'></div>富期润屋。贪以败类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370305_comment'></div>孤汉主析圭之恩。夺苍梧易米之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370305_comment'></div>滥源既启。真质斯閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370305_comment'></div>从予旧而不瑕。谅天视兮有自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370305_comment'></div>孟君来止。惠政潜施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370305_comment'></div>欲不欲之欲。为无为之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370305_comment'></div>不召其珠。珠无胫而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370305_comment'></div>不移其俗。俗如影之随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370305_comment'></div>尔其状也。上掩星彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370305_comment'></div>遥迷月规。粲粲离离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370305_comment'></div>与波逶迤。乍入潭心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370305_comment'></div>时依浦口。惊泉客之初泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370305_comment'></div>疑冯夷之始剖。依于仁里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370305_comment'></div>天亦何言。富彼贪夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370305_comment'></div>神之所不。沙下兮泥閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370305_comment'></div>韬光而自闲。映石华之皎皎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370305_comment'></div>杂鱼目之𩻴𩻴。岂比黄帝之使罔象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370305_comment'></div>元珠乃得。蔺生之诡秦主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370305_comment'></div>荆玉斯还。由是发润洲蘋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370305_comment'></div>增辉岸草。水容益媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370305_comment'></div>泽气弥好。川实效珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370305_comment'></div>地宁爱宝。隐见谅符乎龙跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370305_comment'></div>亏全非系乎蚌老。岂惟彰太守之深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370305_comment'></div>所以表天子之至道。观夫杲耀外澈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370305_comment'></div>英华内含。饰君之履兮岂不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370305_comment'></div>照君之车兮岂不堪。犹未遭于采拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370305_comment'></div>尚见滞于江潭。虽旧史之录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370305_comment'></div>与前贤之谈。终思入掬以腾价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370305_comment'></div>愿得书绅而励贪。于惟明时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370305_comment'></div>不贵异物。徒饰表者招累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370305_comment'></div>而握珍者难屈。是珍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370305_comment'></div>居下流而委弃。历终岁而湮郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370305_comment'></div>望高鉴兮闇投。幸馀波之洗拂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370305_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1370305_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_10740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10740?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青云干吕</a><span class='authorDate'>（791年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10740")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_10740_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_10740'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3242, "poem_allusion_10740")'>干吕青云</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4799, "poem_allusion_10740")'>南风</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_10740_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10740'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10740'>郁郁复纷纷，青霄干吕云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10740'>色令天下见，候向管中分。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10740'>远覆无人境，遥彰有德君。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10740'>瑞容惊不散，冥感信稀闻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_10740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_10740'>湛露羞依草，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4799, "poem_sentence_4_10740")'>南风</span>耻带薰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_10740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_10740'>恭惟汉武帝，馀烈尚氛氲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_10740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_10740'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_10740_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='386ff0929f59487c9b0e0d388c0aecb1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("386ff0929f59487c9b0e0d388c0aecb1");'><span id='386ff0929f59487c9b0e0d388c0aecb1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年</a>，29岁</div><div id='386ff0929f59487c9b0e0d388c0aecb1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年</a>　途经长安，受到李景略的热情款待。作品：《为羽林李景略将军进射雁歌表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span><div id='poem_1370355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为羽林李景略将军进射雁歌表</a><span class='authorDate'>（794年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370355")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370355'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370355'>臣某言。伏惟皇帝陛下某月日临御某殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370355_comment'></div>射飞雁一只。应弦而落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370355_comment'></div>欢动宫闱。武畅环卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370355_comment'></div>中谢。臣家世为将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370355_comment'></div>扬声朔野。弧矢之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370355_comment'></div>少尝习焉。每张侯为鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370355_comment'></div>注镞而释。期于必中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370355_comment'></div>十不一二。今则禽飞于青冥之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370355_comment'></div>箭发于倏忽之间。一声劈云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370355_comment'></div>双翼坠地。此皆神授审固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370355_comment'></div>灵扶端直。以成陛下神武之威也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370355_comment'></div>臣才质无取。蒙恩深厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370355_comment'></div>脱剑免冑之馀。辄思撰射雁歌一章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370355_comment'></div>随此上献。诚不敢继抗坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370355_comment'></div>列风雅。姑以抒下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370355_comment'></div>宣上德。附于大武之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370355_comment'></div>而登歌焉。无任欢抃怔营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370355_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1370355_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='872b31172b8c4b66a9ab3a5e2ce151a6_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　本年丧除，征拜右拾遗。疑后又改太常博士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　本年入朝后，时挚友李逢吉亦在朝任职，两人之间当有往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在朝为官。有诗。作品：《社日早出赴祠祭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗补编》之《全唐诗续拾》卷二七。）</span>“何日居三署，终年尾百僚”<span class='inlineComment2'>（此句见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>社日早出赴祠祭</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10704")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_10704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10704'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10704'>满城人尽闲，惟我早开关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10704'>惭被家童问，因何别旧山？<div id='poem_sentence_1_10704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10704'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_10704_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在朝为官。有文。作品：《为右拾遗表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见陈尚君《全唐文补编》下册《全唐文又再补》卷五引《类要》卷一六。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　本年三月前已迁礼部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　在朝为官。有诗。作品：《南宫夜直宿见李给事封题其所下制敕知奏直在东省因以诗寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span>“移石几回敲废印，开箱何处送新图”<span class='inlineComment2'>（此句见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10741' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10741?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10741'>番直同遥夜，严扃限几重。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10741'>青编书白雀<span class='inlineComment2'>（其日敕，鄜州奏白雀，宜付史馆）</span>，黄纸降苍龙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10741'>北极丝纶句，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_10741", 10741, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>东垣</span>翰墨踪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10741'>尚垂玄露点，犹湿紫泥封。<div id='poem_sentence_3_10741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_10741'>炫眼凝仙烛，驰心袅禁钟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_10741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_10741'>定应形梦寐，暂似接音容。<div id='poem_sentence_5_10741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_10741'>玉树春枝动，金樽腊酿醲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_10741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_10741'>在朝君最旧，休浣许过从。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　在朝为官。有文。作品：《贺德音表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span><div id='poem_1370318' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370318' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370318?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺德音表</a><span class='authorDate'>（811年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370318")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370318'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370318'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370318_comment'></div>伏见今月二十八日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370318_comment'></div>普安群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370318_comment'></div>忧济庶士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370318_comment'></div>每念下农艰苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370318_comment'></div>赈红粟而流衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370318_comment'></div>知贪贾滞财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370318_comment'></div>禁青蚨之飞走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370318_comment'></div>千官耸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370318_comment'></div>万国钦闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370318_comment'></div>中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370318_comment'></div>臣闻损有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370318_comment'></div>补不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370318_comment'></div>太上之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370318_comment'></div>敛以轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370318_comment'></div>散其重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370318_comment'></div>哲王之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370318_comment'></div>肇自古昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370318_comment'></div>垂为宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370318_comment'></div>其或法因情迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370318_comment'></div>事与时异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370318_comment'></div>则物力甚屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370318_comment'></div>人心用咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370318_comment'></div>是故书载行之惟艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370318_comment'></div>史称守而勿失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370318_comment'></div>伏惟睿圣文武皇帝陛下绍兴丕图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370318_comment'></div>光启鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370318_comment'></div>勤恤人隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370318_comment'></div>精知化源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370318_comment'></div>以为麦禾虽登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370318_comment'></div>农食犹歉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370318_comment'></div>布帛大贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370318_comment'></div>女工必伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370318_comment'></div>因发生之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370318_comment'></div>下慈惠之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370318_comment'></div>清问疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370318_comment'></div>昭宣令宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370318_comment'></div>严除暴征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370318_comment'></div>令巳逋责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370318_comment'></div>首自京国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370318_comment'></div>达于淮湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370318_comment'></div>三方虽遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370318_comment'></div>如视以宸鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370318_comment'></div>万几诚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370318_comment'></div>皆经于睿心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370318_comment'></div>自然事耕桑者忘四体之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370318_comment'></div>游韨井者乐一朝之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370318_comment'></div>庆共云布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370318_comment'></div>恩随风翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370318_comment'></div>率土之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370318_comment'></div>不胜庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370318_comment'></div>臣等叨逢圣运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370318_comment'></div>预列班荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370318_comment'></div>攀日月之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370318_comment'></div>无能献替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370318_comment'></div>遇云雷之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370318_comment'></div>空荷沾濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370318_comment'></div>捧戴德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370318_comment'></div>不胜抃跃屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1370318_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　母孙氏卒，停官丁母忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=812&endYear=812')">812年</a>　丁母忧，以善居丧闻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=812&endYear=812')">812年</a>　本年，迁葬父承简于京兆府万年县凤栖原，令狐楚自撰墓碑。疑母孙氏亦同时袝葬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=813&endYear=813')">813年</a>　本年服满，除刑部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年</a>　在刑部员外郎任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年</a>　与杨巨源唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年8月</a>　八月，岐阳公主下嫁杜悰，时相礼缺官，楚以本官摄太常博士权充。楚精于礼仪，为宪宗所重。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年10月</a>　十月，擢职方员外郎，知制诰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年</a>　时淮西用兵，同年进士皇甫镈以善于理财为宪宗所宠，楚善笺表制诰，镈与楚善，荐于宪宗。十一月，入充翰林学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=815&endYear=815')">815年11月11日</a>　十一月十一日，赐绯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=815&endYear=815')">815年12月7日</a>　十二月七日，因宰相推荐，转职方郎中知制诰，依前充翰林学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=816&endYear=816')">816年</a>　在职方郎中任，知制诰及内职如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=816&endYear=816')">816年</a>　与杨巨源唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=816&endYear=816')">816年</a>　又与翰林院同僚王涯、张仲素唱和，后三人唱和诗歌编为《三舍人集一卷》，又名《翰林歌词》<br /><a href="javascript: class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10705'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10705'>杨柳黄金穗，梧桐碧玉枝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10705'>春来消息断，早晚是归期<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作时）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10705'></div><div class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_10701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杂曲歌辞 圣明乐<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作圣明乐）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（816年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10701")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_10701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10701'>海浪恬丹徼，边尘靖黑山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10701'>从今万里外，不复镇萧关。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10701'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_10701_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_10713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10713?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春闺思</a><span class='authorDate'>（816年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10713")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_10713_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10713'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10713'>戴胜飞晴野，凌澌下浊河。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10713'>春风楼上望，谁见泪痕多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10713'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_10713_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年2月13日</a>　二月十三日，沈传师、杜元颍分别自左补阙史馆修撰、太常博士入充翰林学士。令狐楚奉诏与沈传师、杜元颍等编撰《元和辨谤略》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年2月24日</a>　二月二十四日，加承旨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　三月二十日，迁中书舍人，依前充翰林承旨学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　奉旨编纂《御览诗》成，进上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年7月</a>　七月，宰相李逢吉与裴度不协，利用群臣纷议罢兵，极力反对裴度讨伐淮西。令狐楚趋附李逢吉，借起草裴度彰义军节度使制书之机，破坏用兵。裴度恐二人内外合势阻挠军事，遂以草制失辞为由，奏罢令狐楚内职，宪宗用其言。作品：《授裴度彰义军节度使制》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span><div id='poem_1370307' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370307' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370307?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授裴度彰义军节度使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（817年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370307")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370307_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370307'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370307'>门下。辅弼之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370307_comment'></div>军国是赖。兴化致理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370307_comment'></div>则秉钧以居。取威成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370307_comment'></div>则分阃而出。所以同君臣之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370307_comment'></div>而一中外之任焉。属者问罪汝南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370307_comment'></div>致诛淮右。盖欲刷其污俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370307_comment'></div>吊彼顽人。虽弃地求生者实繁有徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370307_comment'></div>而婴城执迷者未剪其类。何兽困而犹斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370307_comment'></div>岂鸟穷之无归欤。由是遥听鼓鼙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370307_comment'></div>更张琴瑟。烦我台席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370307_comment'></div>董兹戎旃。朝议大夫守中书侍郎同中书门下平章事飞骑尉赐紫金鱼袋裴度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370307_comment'></div>为时降生。协朕梦卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370307_comment'></div>精辨宣力。坚明纳忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370307_comment'></div>当轴而才谋老成。运筹而智略前定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370307_comment'></div>司其枢务。备知四方之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370307_comment'></div>付以兵要。必得万人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370307_comment'></div>是用祷于上元。择此吉日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370307_comment'></div>带丞相之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1370307", 1370307, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>印绶</span>。所以尊其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370307_comment'></div>赐诸侯之斧钺。所以重其命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370307_comment'></div>尔宜大布清问。恢壮徽猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370307_comment'></div>感励连营。荡平多垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370307_comment'></div>召怀孤疾。字育夷伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370307_comment'></div>况淮西一军。素效忠节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370307_comment'></div>过海赴难。史策上勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370307_comment'></div>建中初攻破襄阳。擒灭崇义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370307_comment'></div>比者胁于凶逆。归命无由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370307_comment'></div>每念前劳。常思安抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370307_comment'></div>所以内辍佐辅。为之师帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370307_comment'></div>实欲保全慰喻。使各得其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370307_comment'></div>尔往钦哉。无越我丕训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370307_comment'></div>可守门下侍郎同中书门下平章事使持节蔡州诸军事兼蔡州刺史。充彰义军节度管内度支营田使申光蔡等州观察处置等使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370307_comment'></div>仍充淮西宣慰处置使。散官勋如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370307_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1370307_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年8月</a>　八月，罢楚翰林学士，出为中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　罢翰林学士前，已阶朝议郎，并赐紫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　令狐楚出院后，其他学士草制常常言不切旨，宪宗观楚所草制诏，思楚之才。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　在翰林院期间，与僧广宣唱和，后结集。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年10月</a>　九月丁未（二十一），李逢吉罢相，出为剑南东川节度使。十月，令狐楚曾参与编纂之《元和辨谤略》书成，沈传师作序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　本年，李廓曾献诗令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　在朝。有诗。作品：《省中直夜对雪寄李师素侍郎》<span /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年</a>　去年三月至今年四月前在中书舍人任上时，与杨巨源、峰上人唱和往来。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8bd3b2e64fc4486f8dfe64098c481e0c_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=820')">819-820年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='8bd3b2e64fc4486f8dfe64098c481e0c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年7月21日</a>　七月，皇甫镈进门下侍郎，荐令狐楚为朝议大夫、守中书侍郎、同中书门下平章事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年10月</a>　十月或稍后，元稹由虢州长史迁膳部员外郎还京，楚久闻元稹诗名，令稹献其旧作，楚读后大为称赏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　时武儒衡有入相之望，儒衡曾上疏论皇甫镈判度支“剥下以媚上”，令狐楚忌之，欲以计沮之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　十二月，令狐楚遂荐狄仁杰之后山南东道节度推官狄兼谟为左拾遗内供奉，自草制辞。在制辞中，楚盛推狄仁杰之功，借武周篡唐事以影射中伤武儒衡。儒衡泣诉于上，宪宗因薄楚之为人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　本年，令狐楚拜相后，曾与皇甫镈共同向宪宗推荐同年进士萧俛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年7月</a>　今年七月至明年七月在相位时，曾荐李隐为集贤校理；又与进士顾非熊、僧道器往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　今明两年楚在相位期间，前河阳节度使乌重胤幕府节度判官刘颇曾以诗投献令狐楚，楚屡吟赏于人前。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　拜相初，有让表。作品：《让中书侍郎表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span><div id='poem_1370332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让中书侍郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370332")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370332'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370332'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370332_comment'></div>臣闻斗筲之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370332_comment'></div>不可持盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370332_comment'></div>腹背之毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370332_comment'></div>安能翔远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370332_comment'></div>是以知进忘退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370332_comment'></div>易象之深戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370332_comment'></div>在宠若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370332_comment'></div>道家之切训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370332_comment'></div>此微臣所以遑遑然久积肝血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370332_comment'></div>衔恩陈露而未得者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370332_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370332_comment'></div>臣代业儒素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370332_comment'></div>心游文史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370332_comment'></div>虽自励巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370332_comment'></div>岂敢发身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370332_comment'></div>始望之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370332_comment'></div>止于中台郎吏外郡牧守而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370332_comment'></div>幸而因缘昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370332_comment'></div>遭遇盛时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370332_comment'></div>振拔群伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370332_comment'></div>骤登台衮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370332_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下钦明御历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370332_comment'></div>睿哲配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370332_comment'></div>华夏宅心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370332_comment'></div>俊贤翘首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370332_comment'></div>方当选众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370332_comment'></div>固合退身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370332_comment'></div>岂意迁于黄阁之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370332_comment'></div>参以紫微之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370332_comment'></div>特出睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370332_comment'></div>不因人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370332_comment'></div>九重所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370332_comment'></div>万殒何答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370332_comment'></div>诚宜建用皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370332_comment'></div>保合太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370332_comment'></div>宏圣功于尧舜之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370332_comment'></div>追恪德于夔龙之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370332_comment'></div>而和羹乏用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370332_comment'></div>覆餗为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370332_comment'></div>空有仰于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370332_comment'></div>实无裨于元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370332_comment'></div>一自叨窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370332_comment'></div>遽经炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370332_comment'></div>跼影兢魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370332_comment'></div>痛心疾首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370332_comment'></div>伏乞鉴其悃款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370332_comment'></div>察其疾羸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370332_comment'></div>赐以冗员。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370332_comment'></div>则大君知人之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370332_comment'></div>永光于典策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370332_comment'></div>微臣妨贤之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370332_comment'></div>将息于庙谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370332_comment'></div>天下幸甚。<div id='poem_sentence_58_1370332_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　拜相期间，有文。作品：《授狄兼谟拾遗制》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span><div id='poem_1370308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授狄兼谟拾遗制</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370308")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370308'>朕听政馀暇。躬览国书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370308_comment'></div>知奸臣擅权之由。见母后窃位之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370308_comment'></div>我国家神器大宝。将遂傅于他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370308_comment'></div>洪惟昊穹。降鉴储祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370308_comment'></div>诞生仁杰。保佑中宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370308_comment'></div>使绝维更张。明辟乃复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370308_comment'></div>宜福冑嗣。与国无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370308_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1370308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年1月13日</a>　正月十三日，令狐楚有事于太清宫，宪宗为之辍朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年闰1月3日</a>　闰正月三日丙午，令狐楚奉遗册，太子李恒于太极殿即帝位，即穆宗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年闰1月4日</a>　四日丁未，皇甫镈以附宦官吐突承璀欲立澧王。穆宗欲诛之，萧俛及宦官救之，遂贬镈崖州司户参军。贬镈后，朝廷议命宰相，令狐楚荐御史中丞萧俛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年闰1月8日</a>　八日辛亥，楚进门下侍郎，萧俛与中书舍人、翰林学士段文昌同时拜相。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　令狐楚因皇甫镈得势，镈被贬后，楚为朝臣所嫉恨。因萧俛入相，无人敢言。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　楚为门下侍郎时，有文。作品：《大唐故朔方灵盐等军州节度副大使知节度事管内支度营田观察处置押蕃落等使银青光禄大夫检校刑部尚书兼灵州大都督府长史御史大夫安定郡王赠尚书左仆射李公（光进）神道碑铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四三。）</span><div id='poem_1370441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大唐故朔方灵盐等军州节度副大使知节度事管内支度营田观察处置押蕃落等使银青光禄大夫检校刑部尚书兼灵州大都督府长史御史大夫安定郡王赠尚书左仆射李公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（820年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370441")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1370441_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1370441'>□安定郡王讳光进字耀卿节制灵武之三年。岁在乙未季夏六月。寝疾于理所。监军使者驿马以闻。皇帝遣中贵人赍尺一书。与御府医药。驰往临视。旬有八日。奄弃厥命。享年五十七矣。制诏丞相御史。罢朝会。加赗赙。然后以左揆之密印画绶。告于第焉。其年。嗣子季元。河东衙前兵马使检校太子宾客兼监察御史。次曰燧元。陈许节度押衙检校太子宾客兼监察御史。次曰毅元。次曰绶元。宣义郎行太原府太原县尉。次曰宗元。次曰吉元。血泣柴立。护裳帷南归太原。越十一年二月己酉。葬我尚书左仆射安定王于太原府东四十里孝敬原。礼也。公之先本阿跌氏。出于南单于左厢十二姓。代有才杰。继为酋师。尝统数千庐落。号别部大人。贞观初。大父贺之率其属来归。太宗制受鸡田州都督。仍充灵武丰州定塞兵马使。大父袭之。无禄早世。先父良臣。开府仪同三司鸡田州刺史充朔方先锋左助兵马使。夫以三叶之忠厚。一门之信谨。宜锡祚允。降生畯贤。公形清而视明。神全而气和。猿臂虬须。山立玉色。赠工部尚书李奉国。公之伯姊。器公于稠人。教之骑射。付以韬略。由是发迹云中。策名太原。始以勇敢从北平王燧战于蒲次。以愿恭事朗宁王。自艮铁于并。或典领先偏。或训齐部伍。公家之事无细大。戎府之务无重轻。缘手风生。过目冰泮。礼部尚书陇西公说待以心膂。奏兼殿中侍御史。工部尚书荥阳公儋仗为爪牙。表兼御史中丞。大司空严公绶择戏下之才。奏兼御史大夫。司徒范公希朝求军中之旧。迁为检校左散骑常侍。古人云。一心可以事百君。于公见之。自时而后。气概昭宣。风声流闻。人望归厚。天心委重。由代州刺史石岭镇北兵马使代北军使超迁工部尚书单于大都护振武节度支度营田观察押蕃落等使。朝家思所以优宠尊异于公者。无所爱焉。八年秋迁为秋官。改拜灵州。进阶至银青。封□于安定。赐姓李氏。列宗籍。追命先君仪同为工部尚书。先夫人史氏为代国太夫人。君臣交感。家国储庆。焜耀充塞。有如是耶。十三年春。介弟忠武军节度等使银青光禄大夫检校司空同中书门下平章事武威郡开国公光颜既平淮夷。秉圭来朝。疏公官伐德善。涕洟见请。以表邱垄。又会故吏御史任夷则条二府政事。上于考功。故得铺陈馨香。追琢琬玉云。惟公□毅直清。洁矩庄明。不为物迁。能以贞胜。忠信之教。自形于心术。孝悌之行。每合于天经。昔国太夫人尝有霜露之疾。公与今司徒左右就养。不脱冠带者累月。其到雁门也。先惠训而后武断。清静之政成。恺悌之化流。𩻴孤遂安。奸盗讫息。贞元中。孝文之心。在宥天下。无何。李郑二帅。相继物故。大司空严公亦用宽和统三军。辕门武人。骄蹇自便。及公之都纪纲也。言词约而必信。号令明而必行。堂皇之上听无哗。大旆之前立无跛。范司徒之东讨常山也。军旅之事。□以咨之。或堑水以绝其归居。或断桥以防其走进。繄君有命。皆我之为。开网竟从于朝旨。改辕无失于戎律。其在振武也。惩边候之不修。黠虏挻灾。我人离落。于是选骑戒期。扬威棱于沙碛。寇皆愕眙。深潜而远遁矣。病公田之不辟。豪家射利。我庚空竭。于是置吏立程。悬信赏于表缀。农皆鼓舞。寒耕而热耘矣。罕羌之豪曰怀荣。曰黑□戕贼攘敚。横于二垂。前后握兵者率不能禁。公乃飞语以速其卸。开恩而怠其意。密声殄力。如取怀中而杀之。风清河湟。威动朔漠。迁之至于灵武。亦犹是也。而加之以勤俭。因之以廉平。夫家之徭有恒经。井地之征有定制。生物滋殖。齐人乐康。利泽四布。淑声一口。时县官加兵蔡人。且三年矣。楚方奏薄技于内庭。雅知将欲徵□于朔方。济师于许□谓肺肝之可见。俾手足以相卫。公亦义形于色。情发于中。或攘臂而言。或投袂而起。岂天缓狡童之戮于终岁也。翌日而公疾。浃旬而公病。不月而公薨。悲夫。信之结于人也深。惠之被于物也久。闻丧而哭于野者雷动。会葬而登于垄者星奔。岂止剺面刺心。辍舂罢市而已。呜呼。黑山虽顺。赤岭犹虞。而耀卿宰木已高。寿宫永闭。怀忠愤者。得不太息而掩涕乎。蔡邕撰有道之碑。自知无愧。范文观武子之墓。可以与归。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1370441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370441'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370441'>天有风霆，是为威刑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1370441'>国之斧钺，用以征伐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1370441'>明明我后，耀武敷文。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1370441'>蟜蟜我王，砥节邀勋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1370441'>昔在偏裨，其道则直。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1370441'>洎司纲纪，其仪不忒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1370441'>一麾出守，十乘启行。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1370441'>藩篱单于，襦裤朔方。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1370441'>心与世同，政由已出。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1370441'>塞上师壮，军中廪实。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1370441'>既宣大忠，宜奏肤公。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1370441'>西戡畎夷，北伐山戎。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1370441'>庆方来兮任方崇，身己灭兮名已空。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1370441'>罕山之南汾水东，白杨黑柏多悲风。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1370441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1370441'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1370441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年闰1月</a>　本月，以令狐楚充宪宗景陵山陵使摄太尉，令撰哀册文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　去年十月或稍后至今年任山陵使期间，楚与元稹唱和颇多。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年2月</a>　二月，加阶太中大夫。时子令狐绪亦以父荫得官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年2月</a>　本月，楚奏请李䎖兼充按行山陵副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年3月</a>　三月，有诗。作品：《三月晦日会李员外座中频以老大不醉见讥因有此赠》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10687' class='_poem'><div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　穆宗赐楚金石凌、红雪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年5月</a>　楚进宪宗哀册文。作品：《进宪宗哀册文状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span>《唐宪宗章武皇帝哀册文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《全唐文》卷五四三。）</span><div id='poem_1370418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370418?labeling=true' "poem_title_1370418")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370418'>右。奉敕令臣撰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370418_comment'></div>臣今撰了。谨连如后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370418_comment'></div>窃以扬先帝无疆之德。荐陛下罔极之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370418_comment'></div>宜择能者。永垂不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370418_comment'></div>圣意以臣备位相府。策名文场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370418_comment'></div>忘其庸虚。赐以撰述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370418_comment'></div>顷自哀迷重謺。心绪摧落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370418_comment'></div>虽磨铅雕朽。已竭其精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370418_comment'></div>捧日窥天。难穷其高远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370418_comment'></div>干冒封进。无任悲跃屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370418_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1370418_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐宪宗章武皇帝哀册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（820年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370442")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370442'>维元和十五年岁次庚子正月甲戌朔二十七日庚子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370442_comment'></div>移殡于大内太极殿之西阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370442_comment'></div>粤五月十五日庚申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370442_comment'></div>迁座于景陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370442_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370442_comment'></div>玉衡南指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370442_comment'></div>金波西落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370442_comment'></div>皓雪集其麻衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370442_comment'></div>素云褰其绡幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370442_comment'></div>柳宫龙动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370442_comment'></div>竹池鱼跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370442_comment'></div>兆庶雨泣于浩穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370442_comment'></div>万灵风号于寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370442_comment'></div>哀子嗣皇帝仰攀雕辇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370442_comment'></div>殷奠琼筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370442_comment'></div>哀无容以触地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370442_comment'></div>痛不返而终天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370442_comment'></div>仙仗徐进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370442_comment'></div>宸仪永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370442_comment'></div>降睿旨于鸾台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370442_comment'></div>扬圣功于凤册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370442_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370442_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1370442'>配天维唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370442_comment'></div>伊祁同光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370442_comment'></div>应道为帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370442_comment'></div>元元之系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370442_comment'></div>圣人有作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370442_comment'></div>孝子善继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370442_comment'></div>显赫十朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370442_comment'></div>总齐四裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370442_comment'></div>执其大象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370442_comment'></div>司彼左契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370442_comment'></div>武烈诞敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370442_comment'></div>文明下济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370442_comment'></div>出潜离隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370442_comment'></div>或跃未融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370442_comment'></div>亲则盘石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370442_comment'></div>封殊剪桐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370442_comment'></div>承祧黄屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370442_comment'></div>主鬯青宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370442_comment'></div>礼乐尽在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370442_comment'></div>讴歌荐至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370442_comment'></div>轩皇勌勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370442_comment'></div>传付神器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370442_comment'></div>太母侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370442_comment'></div>亲临宝位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370442_comment'></div>怡声下色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370442_comment'></div>先意承志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370442_comment'></div>家令敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370442_comment'></div>天子屏贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370442_comment'></div>明明出震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370442_comment'></div>业业承乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370442_comment'></div>其仁如山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370442_comment'></div>其智如泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370442_comment'></div>理析坚白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370442_comment'></div>学探幽元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370442_comment'></div>挥毫雾动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370442_comment'></div>掞藻霞鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370442_comment'></div>所持者俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370442_comment'></div>所宝者贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370442_comment'></div>刑靡不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370442_comment'></div>赏无不延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370442_comment'></div>冕旒迎日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370442_comment'></div>圭璧祈年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370442_comment'></div>涕谒宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1370442_comment'></div>臣朝昊天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1370442_comment'></div>天纵神圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1370442_comment'></div>日跻孝敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1370442_comment'></div>鸿名再加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1370442_comment'></div>宝历一定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1370442_comment'></div>穷人屡赈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1370442_comment'></div>名士交聘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1370442_comment'></div>兽爱触邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1370442_comment'></div>草怜指佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1370442_comment'></div>梯航修贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1370442_comment'></div>鳞羽遂性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1370442_comment'></div>河色呈符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1370442_comment'></div>山声告庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1370442_comment'></div>编书辩谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1370442_comment'></div>创殿思政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1370442_comment'></div>甘节必称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1370442_comment'></div>苦言终听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1370442_comment'></div>棱威之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1370442_comment'></div>德政之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1370442_comment'></div>霜雪宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1370442_comment'></div>风雷号令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1370442_comment'></div>夏台齿剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1370442_comment'></div>上党纳阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1370442_comment'></div>赵际宅心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1370442_comment'></div>邺中听命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1370442_comment'></div>谁能去兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1370442_comment'></div>王者有征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1370442_comment'></div>玉垒雾廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1370442_comment'></div>金陵镜清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1370442_comment'></div>狐鸣上蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1370442_comment'></div>蚁聚东平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1370442_comment'></div>伏锧就戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1370442_comment'></div>回戈受烹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1370442_comment'></div>始以止杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1370442_comment'></div>归于好生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1370442_comment'></div>恢恢不失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1370442_comment'></div>荡荡难名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1370442_comment'></div>信及隐微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1370442_comment'></div>道存溥博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1370442_comment'></div>走马斯郤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1370442_comment'></div>昆虫咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1370442_comment'></div>调其玉烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1370442_comment'></div>徇以木铎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1370442_comment'></div>混同车书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1370442_comment'></div>远颁正朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1370442_comment'></div>范金合土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1370442_comment'></div>大兴太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1370442_comment'></div>清跸鸣銮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1370442_comment'></div>将登高岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1370442_comment'></div>四维既张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1370442_comment'></div>五刃已藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1370442_comment'></div>蛮夷戎羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1370442_comment'></div>敢不来王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1370442_comment'></div>天下清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1370442_comment'></div>朝廷乐康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1370442_comment'></div>会冠剑以高宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1370442_comment'></div>戏鱼龙于广场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1370442_comment'></div>有严有翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1370442_comment'></div>无怠无荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1370442_comment'></div>俗皆臻于寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1370442_comment'></div>人自为于羲皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1370442_comment'></div>日出入兮安穷极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1370442_comment'></div>云飞扬兮无处所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1370442_comment'></div>瑞方瞻乎凤来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1370442_comment'></div>灾忽闻于鹳语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1370442_comment'></div>谓百年之可卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1370442_comment'></div>嗟九龄之不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1370442_comment'></div>当凝旒而下临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1370442_comment'></div>奄脱屣以轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1370442_comment'></div>万姓哀其考丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1370442_comment'></div>千官怀其后抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1370442_comment'></div>封人犹祝于南山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1370442_comment'></div>帝子已号于北渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1370442_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1370442_comment'></div>披灵衣兮如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1370442_comment'></div>委仙佩兮若休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1370442_comment'></div>建环海以静寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1370442_comment'></div>谢鼎湖而远游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1370442_comment'></div>桂华朗兮高殿寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1370442_comment'></div>梧叶暗兮深宫愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1370442_comment'></div>惊同轨之遽至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1370442_comment'></div>咽长川而不流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1370442_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1370442_comment'></div>威仪肃设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1370442_comment'></div>文物前列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1370442_comment'></div>酌玉斝以宵奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1370442_comment'></div>驾金根而晓发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1370442_comment'></div>出朱雀之正门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1370442_comment'></div>背青鸾之迥阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1370442_comment'></div>逶迤原野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1370442_comment'></div>苍茫日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1370442_comment'></div>去复去兮降尧阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1370442_comment'></div>悲莫悲矣临禹穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1370442_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1370442_comment'></div>地开苍谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1370442_comment'></div>天作丰山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1370442_comment'></div>江海自流于泉下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1370442_comment'></div>城郭取象乎人閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1370442_comment'></div>高封马鬣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1370442_comment'></div>永秘龙颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1370442_comment'></div>鳞有逆兮曾触。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1370442_comment'></div>髯欲升兮高攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1370442_comment'></div>朝百灵以肃肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1370442_comment'></div>遗八骏以闲闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1370442_comment'></div>陵植柏兮未拱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1370442_comment'></div>阁生苔兮已斑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1370442_comment'></div>严日宫而深闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1370442_comment'></div>蔼云幄以空还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1370442_comment'></div>兴众感于万井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1370442_comment'></div>结宸悲于九关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1370442_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1370442_comment'></div>神行无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1370442_comment'></div>乾健不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1370442_comment'></div>物皆被于圣泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1370442_comment'></div>人自迷于帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1370442_comment'></div>巍乎高代之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1370442_comment'></div>至矣动天之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1370442_comment'></div>后元壤以长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1370442_comment'></div>冠苍穹而罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1370442_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_184_1370442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年5月</a>　楚有谢宣行哀册文。作品：《谢宣行哀册文状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span><div id='poem_1370390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢宣行哀册文状</a><span class='authorDate'>（820年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370390")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370390'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370390_comment'></div>臣先准敕撰成封进讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370390_comment'></div>奉某月日敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370390_comment'></div>敬依典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370390_comment'></div>无任号慕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370390_comment'></div>伏以范天地之大者难为状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370390_comment'></div>镌金石之坚者难为工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370390_comment'></div>况先皇之武烈文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370390_comment'></div>迥超前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370390_comment'></div>而微臣之瞽言懵学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370390_comment'></div>不及中人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370390_comment'></div>顾惟庸虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370390_comment'></div>谬获纪述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370390_comment'></div>叨蒙恩奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370390_comment'></div>特赐宣行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370390_comment'></div>窃文士之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370390_comment'></div>诚有惭色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370390_comment'></div>彰圣人之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370390_comment'></div>实荷经纶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1370390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年6月</a>　六月，景陵毕工。放免京兆府本年夏青苗钱，命楚以修山陵剩余绫绢，估价支付京兆府，充代青苗钱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　令狐楚以修山陵功，得赐一子官职，楚以子官回授于弟令狐定。时定任京兆府蓝田县尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　祖崇亮赠吏部尚书，父承简赠礼部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　楚任山陵使期间，手下亲吏韦正牧、于翚等人隐瞒官钱，刻剥工徒，以所得充羡余上献。山陵事毕，为人告发。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　出为宣歙观察使前，勋官已至上轻车都尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年7月27日</a>　七月二十七日丁卯，令狐楚坐此罢相，出为宣歙池观察使。作品：《谢除宣歙观察使表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span><div id='poem_1370335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除宣歙观察使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（820年7月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370335")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370335'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370335'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370335_comment'></div>伏奉今月日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370335_comment'></div>授臣宣州刺史兼御史大夫充宣歙池等州观察处置等使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370335_comment'></div>命自九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370335_comment'></div>恩加一介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370335_comment'></div>兢惶感惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370335_comment'></div>无地自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370335_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370335_comment'></div>臣本以凡材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370335_comment'></div>从来孤立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370335_comment'></div>谬居要地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370335_comment'></div>常积忧危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370335_comment'></div>顷者陛下严奉园陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370335_comment'></div>孝思弓剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370335_comment'></div>微臣职当营护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370335_comment'></div>理合励精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370335_comment'></div>而昧于堤防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370335_comment'></div>误有任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370335_comment'></div>既招牒诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370335_comment'></div>合抵宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370335_comment'></div>岂意陛下恩过生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370335_comment'></div>念深簪履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370335_comment'></div>宽朝廷之典制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370335_comment'></div>委藩镇之赋舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370335_comment'></div>飞魂再还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370335_comment'></div>战汗交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370335_comment'></div>誓当饮冰食蘖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370335_comment'></div>镂骨铭肌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370335_comment'></div>冀申丝发之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370335_comment'></div>上报乾坤之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370335_comment'></div>不胜感恩惶恐屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1370335_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b9b0597d7d744415980c91f8d52a8b9d_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=828&endYear=828')">828年</a>　令狐楚抵长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=828&endYear=828')">828年</a>　拜户部尚书，进爵彭阳县开国侯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=828&endYear=828')">828年</a>　楚归京后，与白居易、刘禹锡当有往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　春，在户部尚书任。与裴度、刘禹锡、白居易、张籍等人唱和往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　在户部尚书任上，窦巩时任司勋员外郎，判度支，两人颇多唱和。作品：《和寄窦七中丞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10736?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鄂州使至窦七副使中丞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>见示与元<sup class='reference id='poem_note_10736_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年3月</a>　本年春，在长安时有诗。作品：《立春后言怀招汴州李匡衙推》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见于《全唐诗》卷三三四。白居易作《送东都留守令狐尚书赴任》（《白居易集》卷二）；刘禹锡作《同乐天送令狐相公赴东都留守（原注：自户部尚书拜）》，见《刘禹锡集》卷三一；张籍作《送令狐尚书赴东都留守》，见《全唐诗》卷三八五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　三月，出为东都留守，白居易、刘禹锡、张籍赋诗送行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　楚赴东都留守时，有诗。作品：《赴东都别牡丹》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10720' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10720")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_10720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10720'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10720'>十年不见小庭花，紫萼临开又别家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10720'>上马出门回首望，何时更得到京华。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10720'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_10720_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='24af4b97943044229e31071678aedcb7_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=836')">833-836年</a>，68-71岁</div><div id='24af4b97943044229e31071678aedcb7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年7月</a>　七月，至长安。唐例，检校官品级高于本官，则从检校官所在朝班。右仆射为二品，吏部尚书为三品，楚以三品不宜居二品之列，固辞。文宗优诏褒许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　时因天旱，文宗命令狐楚等疏决囚犯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　九月，以令狐楚为较内官考使，考核官吏政绩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　今年二月至明年十月，李德裕任宰相期间，曾就元和中令狐楚等所编《元和辨谤略》十卷删其繁芜，增以唐事，编成《大和辨谤略》三卷上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=834&endYear=834')">834年</a>　在吏部尚书任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=834&endYear=834')">834年5月</a>　五月，修奉太庙毕，楚奉命以本官摄太尉举行祭祀典礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=834&endYear=834')">834年</a>　李商隐有上令狐楚状，答谢楚惠借太原任上所著诗歌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=834&endYear=834')">834年</a>　本年前后，改检校尚书左仆射，楚以左仆射位在右仆射之上，固让，文宗优诏许之，仍以检校右仆射兼吏部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　至迟至本年四月时，长子绪已官侍御史，次子绹已迁右拾遗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年6月</a>　六月，令狐楚转太常卿，仍检校尚书右仆射。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年10月</a>　十月，拜尚书左仆射，封彭阳郡公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　在长安，居于开化坊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年11月</a>　十一月，楚以左仆射复判太常卿事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年11月</a>　十一月“甘露之变”，文宗夜诏令狐楚议事禁中，楚不满宦官擅权，同情王涯等人之举，草制叙其罪状浮泛，为宦官仇士良所忌。文宗本欲相楚，至是未果。郑覃、李石相次拜相，楚以本官领诸道盐铁转运榷茶使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　弟令狐定本年迁驾部郎中，充弘文馆直学士。甘露事变时，定往贺新除河东节度使王璠之子王遐休就任弘文馆职，为神策军所系，寻获释。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年12月</a>　十二月，楚复以榷茶不利于民，奏废榷茶使，罢榷茶法，仍由盐铁使主管，实行由产地州县收税的办法，由政府承认的茶商转运贩卖，最后茶税统一上缴户部。文宗从其议。作品：《请罢榷茶使奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span><div id='poem_1370357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢榷茶使奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（835年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370357")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370357'>伏以江淮閒数年已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370357_comment'></div>水旱疾疫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370357_comment'></div>凋伤颇甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370357_comment'></div>愁叹未平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370357_comment'></div>今夏及秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370357_comment'></div>稍较丰稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370357_comment'></div>方须惠恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370357_comment'></div>各使安存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370357_comment'></div>昨者忽奏榷茶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370357_comment'></div>实为蠹政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370357_comment'></div>盖是王涯破灭将至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370357_comment'></div>怨怒合归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370357_comment'></div>岂有令百姓移茶树就官场中栽植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370357_comment'></div>摘茶叶于官场中造作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370357_comment'></div>有同儿戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370357_comment'></div>不近人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370357_comment'></div>方在恩权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370357_comment'></div>孰敢沮议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370357_comment'></div>朝班相顾而失色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370357_comment'></div>道路仄目而吞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370357_comment'></div>今宗社降灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370357_comment'></div>奸凶尽戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370357_comment'></div>圣明垂祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370357_comment'></div>黎庶合安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370357_comment'></div>微臣伏蒙天恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370357_comment'></div>兼领使务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370357_comment'></div>官衔之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370357_comment'></div>犹带此名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370357_comment'></div>俯仰若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370357_comment'></div>夙宵知愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370357_comment'></div>伏乞特回圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370357_comment'></div>下鉴愚诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370357_comment'></div>速委宰臣除此使额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370357_comment'></div>缘军国之用或阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370357_comment'></div>山泽之利有遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370357_comment'></div>许臣条疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370357_comment'></div>续具闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370357_comment'></div>采造将及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370357_comment'></div>妨废为虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370357_comment'></div>前月二十一日内殿奏对之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370357_comment'></div>郑覃与臣同陈论讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370357_comment'></div>伏望圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370357_comment'></div>早赐处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370357_comment'></div>一依旧法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370357_comment'></div>不用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1370357", 1370357, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>新条</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370357_comment'></div>唯纳榷之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370357_comment'></div>须节级加价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370357_comment'></div>商人转卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370357_comment'></div>必较稍贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370357_comment'></div>即是钱出万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370357_comment'></div>利归有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370357_comment'></div>既无害茶商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370357_comment'></div>又不扰茶户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370357_comment'></div>上以彰陛下爱人之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370357_comment'></div>下以竭微臣忧国之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370357_comment'></div>远近传闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370357_comment'></div>必当感悦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1370357_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　又奏请停罢节度使带兵仗入尚书省面辞新例。作品：《奏节度使等带器仗就尚书省参辞状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span><div id='poem_1370434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370434' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏节度使等带器仗就尚书省参辞状</a><span class='authorDate'>（835年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370434")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370434_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370434'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370434'>诸道新授方镇节度使等。具弩抹带器仗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370434_comment'></div>就尚书省兵部参辞。伏以军国异容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370434_comment'></div>古今定制。若不繇旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370434_comment'></div>斯为改常。未闻省閤之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370434_comment'></div>忽入弓刀之器。郑注外蒙恩宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370434_comment'></div>内蓄凶狂。首创奸谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370434_comment'></div>将兴乱兆。遂致王璠郭行馀之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370434_comment'></div>敢驱将吏。直诣阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370434_comment'></div>震惊乘舆。骚动京国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370434_comment'></div>血溅朝路。尸僵禁街。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370434_comment'></div>史册未书。人神共愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370434_comment'></div>既往不咎。其源尚开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370434_comment'></div>前件事宜。伏乞圣恩速令停罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370434_comment'></div>如须参谢。即具公服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370434_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1370434_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年1月</a>　正月大赦，放免京兆府一年租赋，命盐铁使令狐楚以绫绢代还。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　楚奏请以罢修曲江亭绢帛修缮尚书省。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年2月</a>　二月，蔡京因令狐楚荐举，进士及第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年3月</a>　三月上巳节，文宗赐群臣宴曲江。楚以王涯等人新诛，不宜宴乐，独称疾不往。又奏请收敛王涯等人遗骨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　去年十月至今年四月在左仆射任上，时刘禹锡任同州刺史，相距甚近却无从相会，常形于诗歌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　甘露之变后，令狐楚累次上表请辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　四月廿日，楚有文。作品：《大唐回元观钟楼铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见吴钢《全唐文补遗》第一辑。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年4月25日</a>　四月二十五日，令狐楚检校左仆射，出为山南西道节度使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　刘禹锡自同州寄诗送行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　楚赴山南西道节度使任，自长安出发。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
太原
-----detail

class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370342_comment'></div>会从吏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370342_comment'></div>伏赖陛下圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370342_comment'></div>乃得全活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370342_comment'></div>既而肩随多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370342_comment'></div>掌领孤儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370342_comment'></div>警夜巡昼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370342_comment'></div>庶将终老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370342_comment'></div>跼天蹐地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370342_comment'></div>誓不违远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370342_comment'></div>岂意陛下不量臣之能否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370342_comment'></div>拔自近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370342_comment'></div>贰于大藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370342_comment'></div>兴王大都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370342_comment'></div>哓嚣五氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370342_comment'></div>合沓万室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370342_comment'></div>动见指视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370342_comment'></div>甚难为理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>　本年或明年，令狐楚应李说辟请，入河东幕府任掌书记。<br /><a href="javascript:
