ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=796')">796年9月</a>　九月，李景略为节度使李说所忌，出为丰州刺史、兼御史大夫、天德军西受降城都防御使。欲辟令狐楚为从事，值楚婚娶在本月，又因父在太原，故未应景略招请。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>　在李说幕府。时兼任太原府功曹参军，带试弘文馆校书郎衔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>　在太原李说幕府。有文。作品：《贺剑南奏破吐蕃表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span>《为人作请行军司马及少尹状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span><div id='poem_1370325' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370325' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370325?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺剑南奏破吐蕃表</a><span class='authorDate'>（797年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370325")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370325'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370325'>臣某言。当道进奏院状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370325_comment'></div>六月某日剑南节度使韦皋状奏。破吐蕃五千馀众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370325_comment'></div>生擒大酋官七人。阵上杀一百五十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370325_comment'></div>收获牛马四百馀头疋。器械一千五百馀事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370325_comment'></div>吉语远及。欢声相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370325_comment'></div>中贺。臣闻顺实臣道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370325_comment'></div>仗顺者至柔而全。礼为大经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370325_comment'></div>无礼者虽众必败。陛下君临万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370325_comment'></div>天覆兆人。恩覃于幽微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370325_comment'></div>泽及乎荒远。蠢兹蕃丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370325_comment'></div>假息西陲。惟天地含宏之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370325_comment'></div>未能剪灭。以豺狼贪戾之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370325_comment'></div>辄肆陆梁。爰整其师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370325_comment'></div>不攻而取。此皆降睿略于天上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370325_comment'></div>颁明谋于阃外。制士之死命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370325_comment'></div>得人之欢心。所以殪戎如羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370325_comment'></div>破虏若虱。驱彼牛马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370325_comment'></div>获其侯王。威加于殊域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370325_comment'></div>武畅于群动。自然赤山之壤可蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370325_comment'></div>青海之波可涉。必当封土刻石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370325_comment'></div>以垂天声。戎臣司武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370325_comment'></div>获睹其庆。不胜欢抃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370325_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1370325_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370433' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370433' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370433?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人作请行军司马及少尹状</a><span class='authorDate'>（797年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370433")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370433_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370433'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370433'>右。臣适蒙恩奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370433_comment'></div>获守方隅。力小任大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370433_comment'></div>常忧败累。伏以行军司马相副之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370433_comment'></div>知府少尹共理之官。未得其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370433_comment'></div>久空此位。每平均征赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370433_comment'></div>缮理边陲。实藉通材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370433_comment'></div>以分重寄。伏惟陛下察臣心之恳款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370433_comment'></div>知军务之殷繁。选于中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370433_comment'></div>为此副贰。陛下所用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370433_comment'></div>即臣所知。苟获同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370433_comment'></div>庶无阙事。谨遣某官奉状奏请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370433_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1370433_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　在太原李说幕府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　本年前后，长子绪生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　在太原李说幕府。有文。作品：《贺修八陵表毕》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span>《贺灵武破吐蕃表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span>《代李仆射谢子恩赐状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span>《代李仆射谢子恩赐第二状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span>《代李仆射谢子恩赐第三状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span><div id='poem_1370327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370327?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺修八陵毕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370327")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370327'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370327'>臣某言。得进奏院状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370327_comment'></div>八月十五日。百寮于宣政殿贺修八陵毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370327_comment'></div>伏惟陛下行通神明。孝彰天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370327_comment'></div>深怀远慕。严奉诸陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370327_comment'></div>台阶元臣。展敬以祗命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370327_comment'></div>甸服蒸庶。忘劳而陈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370327_comment'></div>薙青芜以疏徼道。扫红腐而净藩园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370327_comment'></div>崇固护于冈陵。增肃清于松柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370327_comment'></div>汉朝充奉。徒见其迁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370327_comment'></div>魏时向望。空闻夫作乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370327_comment'></div>方今大礼。彼实缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370327_comment'></div>天下臣妾。不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370327_comment'></div>况臣名编竹籍。属忝葭莩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370327_comment'></div>感庆之诚。倍百恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370327_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1370327_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺灵武破吐蕃表</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370326")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370326'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370326'>臣某言。臣得朔方节度使李栾牒称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370326_comment'></div>十一月二十日大破吐蕃者。千里喧传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370326_comment'></div>三军快抃。臣某诚欢诚喜顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370326_comment'></div>臣闻天生四夷。用别荒服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370326_comment'></div>国有二柄。谁能去兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370326_comment'></div>伏惟陛下臣妾兆人。庭衢六合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370326_comment'></div>溟波静息。车轨混同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370326_comment'></div>万里清平。三分厎定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370326_comment'></div>而吐蕃膻臊丑类。狂狡阴计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370326_comment'></div>乘陵冻草。妄窃边疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370326_comment'></div>相鼠无牙。安能穿屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370326_comment'></div>羝羊羸角。徒欲触藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370326_comment'></div>是以神圣启其将心。忠勇成于士力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370326_comment'></div>兵既落于天上。虏果陷于彀中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370326_comment'></div>钳口之马。偾车而絷者千蹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370326_comment'></div>辫发之人。为俘舆尸者万指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370326_comment'></div>降旗载路。弃甲满野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370326_comment'></div>遥知水赤。坐想风腥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370326_comment'></div>此皆宗社储灵。朝廷决策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370326_comment'></div>破碎戎胆。振腾天威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370326_comment'></div>凡百人臣。不胜踊跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370326_comment'></div>臣某未申丝发。谬总旗旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370326_comment'></div>欣欢愤激。倍万恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370326_comment'></div>所守有限。不获称庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370326_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1370326_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李仆射谢子恩赐状</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370359")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370359'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370359'>右。臣得进奏院状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370359_comment'></div>中和日伏蒙天恩。赐臣男公敏内宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370359_comment'></div>并赐前件绫罗三十疋银碗一者。臣伏以桃花始开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370359_comment'></div>蓂荚初吐。陛下式崇佳节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370359_comment'></div>以庆仲春。舞八卦于广庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370359_comment'></div>陈四诗于别殿。道光在镐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370359_comment'></div>义冠济汾。盖所以劳徕勋贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370359_comment'></div>昭明慈惠。男公敏年方童幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370359_comment'></div>智乏老成。何殊一芥之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370359_comment'></div>忽宴九天之上。乳口而餐尝鼎食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370359_comment'></div>青衿而陪列朝班。越次之恩已深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370359_comment'></div>踰涯之赐仍及。色丝成疋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370359_comment'></div>烂盈其箱箧。白金为器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370359_comment'></div>皎映于杯盘。泽流而九族皆荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370359_comment'></div>信至而万夫相庆。生子如父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370359_comment'></div>无功则同。知臣者君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370359_comment'></div>报德何日。徘徊官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370359_comment'></div>喜惧交并。戎守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370359_comment'></div>不获陈谢。无任感恩结恋屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370359_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1370359_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=799&endYear=799')">799年</a>　在太原李说幕府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=799&endYear=799')">799年</a>　约于本年，令狐楚受府主之托，令举荐一人可任掌书记之职者，楚以时居太原的前进士齐孝若为荐。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_1370412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>降诞日进银器物及零陵香等状</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370412'>右。伏以千年元命之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370412_comment'></div>四月正阳之气。出震吉日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370412_comment'></div>继乾良辰。黄河再清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370412_comment'></div>冠中古之表德。恒星不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370412_comment'></div>掩西方之诞圣。前件器物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370412_comment'></div>或坚白无玷。或馨香有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370412_comment'></div>敢同率土之心。以续如天之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370412_comment'></div>干冒宸扆。伏增战越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370412_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1370412_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370413?labeling=true' target='_blank'>降诞日进鞍马等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（799年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370413'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370413'>右。臣伏以绕枢之电。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370413_comment'></div>曾委瑞于轩皇。照室之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370413_comment'></div>昔呈祥于汉后。伏惟皇帝陛下贵从天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370413_comment'></div>明在日中。当四月之正阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370413_comment'></div>值千秋之圣运。人神叶庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370413_comment'></div>朝野同欢。臣任重戎旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370413_comment'></div>路遥北阙。欢呼万岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370413_comment'></div>如闻山岳之声。倾竭一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370413_comment'></div>庶均葵藿之志。前件马等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370413_comment'></div>诚非珍异。颇似柔驯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370413_comment'></div>干冒宸严。伏增战越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370413_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1370413_comment'></div></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370330'>臣某言。得进奏院状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370330_comment'></div>义章公主今月九日薨。辍朝七日者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370330_comment'></div>臣伏闻公主分辉帝籍。擢秀皇闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370330_comment'></div>丽有掩于舜华。才成下嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370330_comment'></div>庆初传于螽羽。奄有上仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370330_comment'></div>伏惟陛下仁爱方深。恩慈所属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370330_comment'></div>始其凋谢。轸以悲伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370330_comment'></div>臣限守边陲。忝联枝叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370330_comment'></div>不获陪位奉慰。无任哀塞悽怆恋结之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370330_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1370330_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1370429_comment'></div>臣伏以吴少诚内怀奸诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370429_comment'></div>上负圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370429_comment'></div>因幸邻丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370427_comment'></div>作为奸乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370427_comment'></div>尚延晷刻之命。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370427_comment'></div>惟恐不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370427_comment'></div>况将士等忠义居心。<div class='inline' showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为太原李说尚书进白兔状</a><span class='authorDate'>（796年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a id='poem_sentence_3_1370422_comment'></div>臣谨按瑞应图曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370422_comment'></div>白兔寿千年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370422_comment'></div>满五百则色白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370422_comment'></div>又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370422_comment'></div>王者恩加耆老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370422_comment'></div>则白兔见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370422_comment'></div>臣伏以白惟正色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370422_comment'></div>兔实仁兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370422_comment'></div>来皆有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370422_comment'></div>出必以时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370422_comment'></div>伏惟陛下圣寿无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370422_comment'></div>神功不宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370422_comment'></div>是故太阴精魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370422_comment'></div>降以为瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370422_comment'></div>皓质玉立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370422_comment'></div>素毛霜垂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370422_comment'></div>清明不让于殷狼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370422_comment'></div>皎洁可齐于周鹿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370386_comment'></div>长皆被土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370386_comment'></div>贵实兼金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370386_comment'></div>谨并捧受分给讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370386_comment'></div>所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370386_comment'></div>不获陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370386_comment'></div>无任感庆屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1370386_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（799年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370387")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370387'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370387'>右。中使某至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370387_comment'></div>伏奉敕书手诏。慰问臣及将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370387_comment'></div>兼宣恩旨。赐臣等前件冬衣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370387_comment'></div>伏以纶綍之言。出于天泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370387_comment'></div>衣裳之受。必以王功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370387_comment'></div>臣职在总戎。任当平寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370387_comment'></div>效无丝发。非圣主而岂容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370387_comment'></div>施若邱山。在愚臣而将压。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370387_comment'></div>今者司寒肇至。命服载新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370387_comment'></div>降自九霄。来经千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370387_comment'></div>错鸟章于襟带。奋龙文于素笺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370387_comment'></div>兼并缛丽。备极瑰奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370387_comment'></div>木石之姿。过蒙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1370387", 1370387, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>鲜饰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370387_comment'></div>冰霜之气。顿减严凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370387_comment'></div>曳娄而贱质生光。愤悱而懦心增勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370387_comment'></div>终期薄效。用答深恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370387_comment'></div>谨准敕受兼分给诸将讫。所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370387_comment'></div>不获陈谢。无任感戴之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370387_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1370387_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第三状</a><span class='authorDate'>（799年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370388")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370388'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370388'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370388_comment'></div>中使吴千金至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370388_comment'></div>伏奉敕书手诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370388_comment'></div>慰问臣及将士等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370388_comment'></div>并宣恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370388_comment'></div>赐臣冬衣两副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370388_comment'></div>及诸将衣二十副者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370388_comment'></div>臣守国之藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370388_comment'></div>荷天之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370388_comment'></div>名声绩用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370388_comment'></div>未有可称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370388_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下仁育四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370388_comment'></div>泽均群动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370388_comment'></div>当元律开冬之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370388_comment'></div>念祁寒用事之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370388_comment'></div>书诏交飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370388_comment'></div>衣裘叠至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370388_comment'></div>墨尽龙蛇之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370388_comment'></div>绫兼龟鹤之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370388_comment'></div>服玩而衰残有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370388_comment'></div>拊循而孱懦增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370388_comment'></div>自臣而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370388_comment'></div>万口一声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370388_comment'></div>臣并准敕分配讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370388_comment'></div>不胜欢抃愧恋之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1370388_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为楼烦监杨大夫请朝觐表</a><span class='authorDate'>（799年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370351")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370351'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370351'>臣某言。臣闻君犹父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370351_comment'></div>臣犹子也。子事父有冬温夏凊之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370351_comment'></div>臣事君有大聘小聘之义。臣虽庸鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370351_comment'></div>尝感斯言。况乃地离京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370351_comment'></div>千里而近。身去王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370351_comment'></div>十年有馀。心既倾而阳光未回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370351_comment'></div>目巳极而云路犹阻。此臣所以形留神往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370351_comment'></div>泪尽血继者也。况监司之寄甚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370351_comment'></div>马乘之务非细。或物有因袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370351_comment'></div>革之而无妨。或事无典据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370351_comment'></div>为之而有利。咸非翰墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370351_comment'></div>所可升闻。贮于中心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370351_comment'></div>期以上达。伏惟陛下回天地之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370351_comment'></div>垂日月之明。俯借恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370351_comment'></div>暂令朝奏。傥得飞缨于赤墀之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370351_comment'></div>委佩于彤庭之前。目见龙颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370351_comment'></div>足履丹地。则犬马大幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370351_comment'></div>与天无穷。无任悃款之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370351_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1370351_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>降诞日为杨大夫奏修功德并进马状</a><span class='authorDate'>（799年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370417")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370417'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370417_comment'></div>臣伏以居至道之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370417_comment'></div>其唯元命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370417_comment'></div>助无疆之祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370417_comment'></div>亦在胜因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370417_comment'></div>是以千年为庆诞之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370417_comment'></div>百福有庄严之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370417_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下以文武道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370417_comment'></div>为天人师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370417_comment'></div>降生于纯阳之月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370417_comment'></div>缵承于大宝之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370417_comment'></div>效祉而四夷奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370417_comment'></div>流欢而万国讴歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370417_comment'></div>臣某职在监司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370417_comment'></div>土无珍异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370417_comment'></div>恨无以拜上元之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370417_comment'></div>酬厚载之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370417_comment'></div>敢伏普通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370417_comment'></div>转修经戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370417_comment'></div>仰申诚恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370417_comment'></div>以就有为之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370417_comment'></div>上为圣神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370417_comment'></div>庶资无量之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370417_comment'></div>其马久令教习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370417_comment'></div>颇似柔驯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370417_comment'></div>愿承内厩之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370417_comment'></div>以备属车之驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370417_comment'></div>干冒尘渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370417_comment'></div>不任战汗之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1370417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　仍在李说幕府。楚在太原幕府所撰表奏为德宗所称赏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　在李说幕府，同僚可考者有齐孝若、薛芳、李光进、刘胜孙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年10月</a>　十月，李说卒，行军司马郑儋检校工部尚书，充河东节度使。作品：《为人作奏贬晋阳县主簿姜鉥状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span><div id='poem_1370432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人作奏贬晋阳县主簿姜鉥状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370432")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370432'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370432'>右。臣刘氏堂外生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370432_comment'></div>即故硖州刺史伯华嫡孙。左补阙某第三女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370432_comment'></div>是臣亡叔庶子绛州刺史勋外孙。父身早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370432_comment'></div>臣妹多病。遗孤寡妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370432_comment'></div>无所依投。及臣总戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370432_comment'></div>来相依止。臣见其长成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370432_comment'></div>须有从归。其姜鉥久在太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370432_comment'></div>曾任主簿。诚非匹敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370432_comment'></div>误与婚姻。岂料如兽之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370432_comment'></div>同人之面。纵横凶悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370432_comment'></div>举止颠狂。旬月之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370432_comment'></div>豪横备极。恶言丑语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370432_comment'></div>所不忍闻。有忝祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370432_comment'></div>难施面目。臣以为夫妇之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370432_comment'></div>无义则离。因遣作书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370432_comment'></div>遂令告绝。矜其愚下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370432_comment'></div>拟许生全。而将校等二十三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370432_comment'></div>播进于庭。确论其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370432_comment'></div>具如前列。请以上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370432_comment'></div>虽忍孤儿可欺。其如众怒难息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370432_comment'></div>特希窜谪。以雪冤疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370432_comment'></div>干冒宸扆。伏增战越之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370432_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1370432_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　在太原李说幕府。有文。作品：《为人作奏薛芳充支使状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span>《代李仆射谢赐男绢等物并赠亡妻晋国夫人表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span>《代李仆射谢男赐绯鱼袋表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span>《谢赐腊日口脂红雪紫雪历日等状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span>《为人谢赐男岁节料并口脂蜡脂等状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span>《为人谢问疾状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span>《为人谢问疾兼赐医药等状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span>《为人谢诏书问疾兼赐药方等状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span>《为人作荐刘孟修状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span><div id='poem_1370401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人作奏薛芳充支使状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370401")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370401'>右件官蕴蓄公才。精勤吏道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370401_comment'></div>文章史传。无不该通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370401_comment'></div>大历末则与臣及徐泗节度使张建封同事故马燧作判官。建中三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370401_comment'></div>曾以公事直言。不合其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370401_comment'></div>遂被奏授交城县令。及有政绩褎然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370401_comment'></div>疲羸悉安。征赋皆办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370401_comment'></div>臣以其四居畿令。两任法官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370401_comment'></div>有学有才。堪为宾佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370401_comment'></div>委令推断。无不详平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370401_comment'></div>与之筹画。多所裨益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370401_comment'></div>相谙相识。二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370401_comment'></div>滞屈最深。实希荣奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370401_comment'></div>伏望天恩特赐改官。充臣观察支使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370401_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1370401_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李仆射谢赐男绢等物并赠亡妻晋国夫人表</a><span "poem_title_1370350")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370350'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370350'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370350_comment'></div>臣得进奏院状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370350_comment'></div>三月二十五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370350_comment'></div>本道监军李辅光奉宣进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370350_comment'></div>赐臣男公敏绢五十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370350_comment'></div>衣一副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370350_comment'></div>着盖碗一并合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370350_comment'></div>发遣往东都办护丧事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370350_comment'></div>至二十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370350_comment'></div>伏奉敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370350_comment'></div>赐臣妻博陵郡夫人崔氏晋国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370350_comment'></div>钦承明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370350_comment'></div>以悲以欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370350_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370350_comment'></div>臣某帝枝末属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370350_comment'></div>天壤微生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370350_comment'></div>幸偶升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370350_comment'></div>叨居要剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370350_comment'></div>生成之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370350_comment'></div>无以奉于君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370350_comment'></div>封赏之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370350_comment'></div>岂望及于妻子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370350_comment'></div>今者一门之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370350_comment'></div>二日之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370350_comment'></div>王泽浃于幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370350_comment'></div>天光蟠于高下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370350_comment'></div>受恩过厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370350_comment'></div>忍愧逾深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370350_comment'></div>且剪叶为圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370350_comment'></div>晋封所以称其大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370350_comment'></div>织缣如雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370350_comment'></div>班女由是咏其妍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370350_comment'></div>既耀溢于亲疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370350_comment'></div>实感缠于存殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370350_comment'></div>未知所答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370350_comment'></div>难以自陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370350_comment'></div>空知想泉路以伤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370350_comment'></div>仰天衢而稽首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370350_comment'></div>所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370350_comment'></div>未获陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370350_comment'></div>无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1370350_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李仆射谢男赐绯鱼袋表</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370343")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370343'>臣某言。臣得进奏院状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370343_comment'></div>今月七日。圣慈召臣男公敏令对见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370343_comment'></div>其日中使马承倩奉宣进止。赐绯鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370343_comment'></div>钦承失图。启处无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370343_comment'></div>臣某中谢。臣才非动众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370343_comment'></div>勇不兼人。仰缘枝叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370343_comment'></div>获展筋力。荷天百禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370343_comment'></div>幸据于周诗。遗子一经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370343_comment'></div>诚惭于汉史。男公敏义方未教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370343_comment'></div>容止无仪。伏蒙陛下召入清禁之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370343_comment'></div>立于丹墀之下。远忧颠沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370343_comment'></div>伏用兢惶。岂意明命曲临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370343_comment'></div>荣光下烛。小觿犹佩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370343_comment'></div>忽带金章。褐衣才解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370343_comment'></div>便绾朱绂。生成之功不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370343_comment'></div>浸润之泽无涯。重若戴山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370343_comment'></div>辉如衣锦。匈奴未灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370343_comment'></div>方忍耻于愚臣。童子何知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370343_comment'></div>复蒙恩于圣主。六姻交贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370343_comment'></div>百众同欢。空竭节于边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370343_comment'></div>岂酬仁于覆载。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1370343", 1370343, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>铭肤镂骨</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370343_comment'></div>不敢殒坠。所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370343_comment'></div>不获陈谢。臣无任感激屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370343_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1370343_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐腊日口脂红雪紫雪历日等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370382")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370382'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370382_comment'></div>中使董文萼至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370382_comment'></div>伏奉诏书慰问臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370382_comment'></div>并宣恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370382_comment'></div>赐臣前件物等者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370382_comment'></div>臣伏以天书垂露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370382_comment'></div>御历颁年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370382_comment'></div>灵膏有琼液之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370382_comment'></div>仙散拟雪花之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370382_comment'></div>司天推步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370382_comment'></div>定分至于四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370382_comment'></div>尚药煎和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370382_comment'></div>辨君臣于百品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370382_comment'></div>无不关于睿想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370382_comment'></div>发自宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370382_comment'></div>下锡勋烈之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370382_comment'></div>犹无过分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370382_comment'></div>幸沾庸微之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370382_comment'></div>实所难胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370382_comment'></div>况乏润身之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370382_comment'></div>欣蒙苦口之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370382_comment'></div>谨当奉扬节候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370382_comment'></div>下告于万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370382_comment'></div>宣播光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370382_comment'></div>旁誇于九族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370382_comment'></div>殊私未答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370382_comment'></div>渥泽逾深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370382_comment'></div>夙夜寝兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370382_comment'></div>无任感戴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1370382_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人谢赐男岁节料并口脂腊脂等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370383'>右。臣得男公敏状称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370383_comment'></div>伏奉恩旨。赐岁节料面两石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370383_comment'></div>羊一腔。酒五㪷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370383_comment'></div>口脂腊脂红雪各一合者。臣谬以庸虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370383_comment'></div>叨尘任使。陛下前因蜡日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370383_comment'></div>已降使臣。既沾泽口之膏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370383_comment'></div>又赐雪烦之散。一从捧受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370383_comment'></div>实未遑宁。岂疲病小男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370383_comment'></div>复蒙宠锡。酒浆口腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370383_comment'></div>充溢于杯盘。药饵脂膏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370383_comment'></div>馨香于怀袖。虽君父用赏延之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370383_comment'></div>微细不遗。而臣子非立功之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370383_comment'></div>光辉斯极。岂德泽之私于一物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370383_comment'></div>俾恩波之重若三山。夙夜寝兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370383_comment'></div>以荣为惧。戎守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370383_comment'></div>不获陈谢。无任感庆屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370383_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1370383_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370320' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370320' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370320?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺老人星见表</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370320'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370320'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370320_comment'></div>当道进奏院状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370320_comment'></div>司天台奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370320_comment'></div>八月十五日乙亥夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370320_comment'></div>老人星见于东井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370320_comment'></div>色黄明润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370320_comment'></div>敕旨宣付所司者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370320_comment'></div>率土咸观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370320_comment'></div>际天同庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370320_comment'></div>中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370320_comment'></div>臣闻上天不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370320_comment'></div>而星垂象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370320_comment'></div>次舍隐见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370320_comment'></div>其指甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370320_comment'></div>伏惟陛下道冠帝先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370320_comment'></div>恩覃物表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370320_comment'></div>太和之气上达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370320_comment'></div>万寿之瑞下呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370320_comment'></div>既在东井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370320_comment'></div>又当秦分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370320_comment'></div>色侔蒸栗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370320_comment'></div>光掩连珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370320_comment'></div>彰尔宝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370320_comment'></div>类尧年之河出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370320_comment'></div>延长圣历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370320_comment'></div>齐汉代之山呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370320_comment'></div>凡百臣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370320_comment'></div>欢心如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370320_comment'></div>况臣幸沾皇属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370320_comment'></div>叨守国藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370320_comment'></div>瞻望阙庭不胜庆抃之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1370320_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_1370370_comment'></div>监军李辅光回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370370_comment'></div>伏奉敕书手诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370370_comment'></div>宣慰臣及参佐将校官吏等者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370370_comment'></div>臣窃位大藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370370_comment'></div>连荣近属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370370_comment'></div>戴山之力虽竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370370_comment'></div>横草之功未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370370_comment'></div>寝兴以思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370370_comment'></div>忧愧若厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370370_comment'></div>伏惟陛下日明于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370370_comment'></div>子育其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370370_comment'></div>降玉箸之天书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370370_comment'></div>遣银珰之星使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370370_comment'></div>宸心照育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370370_comment'></div>下浃于将校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370370_comment'></div>慈旨丁宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370370_comment'></div>旁沾于掾吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370370_comment'></div>欢呼之声雷动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370370_comment'></div>舞抃之袖云翻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370370_comment'></div>荣光并临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370370_comment'></div>愁疾如失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370370_comment'></div>不胜欣喜感戴之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1370370_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为崔仲孙弟谢手诏状</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370376'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370376_comment'></div>中使尹偕至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370376_comment'></div>伏奉手诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370376_comment'></div>慰问臣等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370376_comment'></div>伏以圣泽均沾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370376_comment'></div>天光下烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370376_comment'></div>欣荣感戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370376_comment'></div>不胜自任。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1370376_comment'></div>婴孩之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370376_comment'></div>长养于外家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370376_comment'></div>童冠之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370376_comment'></div>因依于伯姊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370376_comment'></div>容身寄食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370376_comment'></div>以至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370376_comment'></div>李说念臣以密亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370376_comment'></div>署臣以散职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370376_comment'></div>誓将裨补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370376_comment'></div>义不依违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370376_comment'></div>诚意莫申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370376_comment'></div>大期俄迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370376_comment'></div>今者获成安泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370376_comment'></div>仰荷圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370376_comment'></div>岂期特降恩波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370376_comment'></div>深蒙慰抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370376_comment'></div>昆虫贱命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370376_comment'></div>不可以戴天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370376_comment'></div>葵藿微心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370376_comment'></div>空知其向日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370376_comment'></div>亲疏共感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370376_comment'></div>存殁同荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370376_comment'></div>无任感恩抃跃之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1370376_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370379' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370379?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人谢问疾状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370379")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370379_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370379'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370379'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370379_comment'></div>监军使李辅光回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370379_comment'></div>奉宣口敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370379_comment'></div>问所疾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370379_comment'></div>臣顷因时旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370379_comment'></div>疾以忧生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370379_comment'></div>仰蒙覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370379_comment'></div>寻就痊除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370379_comment'></div>伏以君恩过厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370379_comment'></div>天听至卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370379_comment'></div>缕形于词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370379_comment'></div>如抚以手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370379_comment'></div>顾惭微细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370379_comment'></div>特系于宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370379_comment'></div>内省疲羸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370379_comment'></div>尚关于睿想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370379_comment'></div>荣深益惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370379_comment'></div>喜极而悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370379_comment'></div>当望双阙以注心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370379_comment'></div>守一隅而尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370379_comment'></div>不胜感结抃跃之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1370379_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人谢问疾兼赐医药等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370377")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370377'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370377'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370377_comment'></div>今月十八日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370377_comment'></div>本道监军使李某至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370377_comment'></div>奉宣口敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370377_comment'></div>问臣所疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370377_comment'></div>十九日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370377_comment'></div>中使张良祐至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370377_comment'></div>伏奉诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370377_comment'></div>赐臣乌药蓼子各一合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370377_comment'></div>药方两纸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370377_comment'></div>并借供奉医官两人医臣疾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370377_comment'></div>臣素是凡庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370377_comment'></div>猥当朝寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370377_comment'></div>暂乖将息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370377_comment'></div>特轸圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370377_comment'></div>纶出王言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370377_comment'></div>朝昏不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370377_comment'></div>星驰驿骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370377_comment'></div>道路相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370377_comment'></div>颁仙药于云中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370377_comment'></div>降神医于天上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370377_comment'></div>仰承荣宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370377_comment'></div>冀即痊平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370377_comment'></div>兢惶失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370377_comment'></div>感戴无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370377_comment'></div>蒲柳之心犹壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370377_comment'></div>誓竭丹诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370377_comment'></div>狗马之齿更长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370377_comment'></div>敢忘元造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370377_comment'></div>臣见准诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370377_comment'></div>与医人商量服饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370377_comment'></div>未及涂药将息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370377_comment'></div>肿气已退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370377_comment'></div>烦热未定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370377_comment'></div>所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370377_comment'></div>不获陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370377_comment'></div>无任感恩结恋之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1370377_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370378?labeling=true' "poem_title_1370378")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370378'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370378'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370378_comment'></div>臣奏事官高荣朝回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370378_comment'></div>伏奉墨诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370378_comment'></div>问臣所疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370378_comment'></div>并奉宣口敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370378_comment'></div>赐臣药方者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370378_comment'></div>臣疲驽之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370378_comment'></div>寒热所侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370378_comment'></div>仰凭天慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370378_comment'></div>今日已损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370378_comment'></div>岂意犹烦睿想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370378_comment'></div>尚轸圣衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370378_comment'></div>特降千金之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370378_comment'></div>兼飞五色之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370378_comment'></div>荣光一烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370378_comment'></div>愁疾如遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370378_comment'></div>誓毕微生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370378_comment'></div>以酬殊造。<div class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人作荐刘孟修状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370400")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370400'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370400_comment'></div>前件业传忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370400_comment'></div>雅尚文儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370400_comment'></div>贞白居心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370400_comment'></div>公勤守职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370400_comment'></div>累曾试用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370400_comment'></div>皆著清廉。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370400_comment'></div>直道不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370400_comment'></div>正词无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370400_comment'></div>宾僚之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370400_comment'></div>裨益甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370400_comment'></div>知是公才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370400_comment'></div>岂为参佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370400_comment'></div>屡详疑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370400_comment'></div>心尽哀矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370400_comment'></div>尝判剧曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370400_comment'></div>事无留滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370400_comment'></div>臣是以录其劳效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370400_comment'></div>奏请改官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370400_comment'></div>伏蒙圣恩特授前件官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370400_comment'></div>今赴阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370400_comment'></div>奉诏旨不敢乞留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370400_comment'></div>臣伏以孟修自有干能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370400_comment'></div>诚堪任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370400_comment'></div>所知微分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370400_comment'></div>辄敢荐闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370400_comment'></div>干冒宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370400_comment'></div>伏增战越。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1370400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　令狐楚入郑儋幕府任掌书记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　在太原郑儋幕府。有文。作品：《贺韩仆射充招讨使状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span>《贺行营破贼状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span>《贺破贼兼优恤将士状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span>《白杨神新庙碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四三。）</span>《揍教习长鎗及弓弩状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span>《为人作谢赐行营将士匹段并设料等物状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span>《为人谢赐行营将士袄子及弓弩状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span>《贺行营破贼状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span>《谢赐衣甲及药物等表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span>《为郑儋尚书谢河东节度使表》<span showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺韩仆射充招讨使状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370395")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370395'>右。中使臣希倩至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370395_comment'></div>伏奉诏书。吴少诚比令招讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370395_comment'></div>都不悛心。今以韩全义充蔡州行营招讨处置等使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370395_comment'></div>臣当军兵马。令取全义指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370395_comment'></div>上官说充招讨副使。令臣使人诣行营所抚慰将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370395_comment'></div>仍令激励。臣伏见逆贼吴少诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370395_comment'></div>残喘微生。骤飞贱品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370395_comment'></div>敢违帝命。来即灵诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370395_comment'></div>陛下天覆为心。云行其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370395_comment'></div>念日月所照。九州攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370395_comment'></div>哀陷阱之中。一夫不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370395_comment'></div>悬申诏旨。开赐生全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370395_comment'></div>而长恶未悛。执迷不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370395_comment'></div>凶逾殛鲧。声极吠尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370395_comment'></div>今既慎选武臣。尽驱猛士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370395_comment'></div>威声先路。实励于震霆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370395_comment'></div>剪灭剋期。必同于沃雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370395_comment'></div>欣欢奋激。倍百恒情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370395_comment'></div>当道应行营将士等。悉怀感怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370395_comment'></div>畜力候奋。指踪示处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370395_comment'></div>既以得人。致命捐躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370395_comment'></div>必应无敌。臣即准诏差人专往慰谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370395_comment'></div>仍切加激励。冀申微效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370395_comment'></div>用答深恩。不任悃款之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370395_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1370395_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺破贼兼优恤将士状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370396")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370396'>右。中使臣希倩至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370396_comment'></div>伏奉诏书。得全义总率诸军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370396_comment'></div>已入贼界。四月二十七日大破贼徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370396_comment'></div>并擒斩生级。如有身死王事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370396_comment'></div>已委全义并给棺榇。送归本道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370396_comment'></div>令臣五年莫停衣粮者。吴少诚畎浍下流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370396_comment'></div>不朝于海。根荄弱质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370396_comment'></div>自绝于天。狴牢之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370396_comment'></div>鸣吠未已。今霜锋云集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370396_comment'></div>月羽风驰。既压贼军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370396_comment'></div>才闻儳鼓。将摩寇垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370396_comment'></div>已见靡旗。实庙堂知先胜之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370396_comment'></div>校队陈争登之力。诛锄有次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370396_comment'></div>蔑杀无难。凡在方隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370396_comment'></div>不胜欣抃。臣伏以虽忠不烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370396_comment'></div>战士所羞。视死如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370396_comment'></div>武夫之志。伏惟陛下宏天覆帱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370396_comment'></div>为日照临。载激怒肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370396_comment'></div>爰收肤骨。汉世徒颁其槥椟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370396_comment'></div>义阙送终。周诗纵裹其糇粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370396_comment'></div>赏延非嗣。以今观古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370396_comment'></div>奋一当千。臣获守边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370396_comment'></div>叨居将帅。无任感激之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370396_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1370396_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白杨神新庙碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370440")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370440'>道太原而北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370440_comment'></div>列郡数十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370440_comment'></div>雁门为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370440_comment'></div>在周秦时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370440_comment'></div>与山戎林胡犬牙其疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370440_comment'></div>国家以文德柔惠而驱去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370440_comment'></div>北迹距塞口犹千里而远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370440_comment'></div>若内地控于通都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370440_comment'></div>秩二千石者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370440_comment'></div>非休勋懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370440_comment'></div>则名王旄士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370440_comment'></div>乙亥岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370440_comment'></div>今尚书陇西李公廉刺并部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370440_comment'></div>选第郡政之尤异者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370440_comment'></div>得昌化守南康郡王河南元韶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370440_comment'></div>首表其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370440_comment'></div>遽闻于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370440_comment'></div>玺书劳勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370440_comment'></div>移理于代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370440_comment'></div>惟南康以壮事老谋逮事先侍中平王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370440_comment'></div>则尚书朗宁王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370440_comment'></div>勤于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370440_comment'></div>惠于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370440_comment'></div>而敬恭于神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370440_comment'></div>由是神降之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370440_comment'></div>人怀其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370440_comment'></div>是岁夏五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370440_comment'></div>赤车彤幨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370440_comment'></div>至自石州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370440_comment'></div>初一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370440_comment'></div>会计于官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370440_comment'></div>察掾吏之勤惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370440_comment'></div>次二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370440_comment'></div>存问于里闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370440_comment'></div>求人民之利病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370440_comment'></div>既三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370440_comment'></div>遍祭于山川神祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370440_comment'></div>盖无停阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370440_comment'></div>銮不辍声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370440_comment'></div>于郡东凡四十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370440_comment'></div>白杨有祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370440_comment'></div>实代之主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370440_comment'></div>嘑水旁注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370440_comment'></div>雁门山前峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370440_comment'></div>磐礡相抵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370440_comment'></div>为堆为阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370440_comment'></div>蘙荟柯条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370440_comment'></div>如虬如龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370440_comment'></div>广仅百亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370440_comment'></div>厥高又倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370440_comment'></div>信可以回薄日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370440_comment'></div>而避逃风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370440_comment'></div>岂朔漠之气凝结于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370440_comment'></div>坤元之精决泄于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370440_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370440_comment'></div>其何以巍巍苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370440_comment'></div>将欲戛若木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370440_comment'></div>稍扶桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370440_comment'></div>卑大椿于漆园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370440_comment'></div>小蟠桃于东方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370440_comment'></div>与夫古墓多悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370440_comment'></div>芜城早落者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370440_comment'></div>不同品矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370440_comment'></div>按诸经记且曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370440_comment'></div>昔元魏高祖孝文帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1370440_comment'></div>由一成而宅九有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1370440_comment'></div>起云中而驭天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1370440_comment'></div>损益三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1370440_comment'></div>宪章百王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1370440_comment'></div>厥初经营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1370440_comment'></div>由此途出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1370440_comment'></div>系马其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1370440_comment'></div>歇鞍于枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1370440_comment'></div>威灵所凭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1370440_comment'></div>别白而在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1370440_comment'></div>既<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1370440", 1370440, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>偃顿</span>以附土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1370440_comment'></div>又跳腾而架空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1370440_comment'></div>如有高掌蹠为鸟势形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1370440_comment'></div>洎今朝中书令燕公说摹咏其事<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1370440_comment'></div>户部侍郎吉公中孚申而明之<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1370440_comment'></div>故迹弥显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1370440_comment'></div>高名益大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1370440_comment'></div>为屏为图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1370440_comment'></div>播于海嵎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1370440_comment'></div>代人神之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1370440_comment'></div>是以祠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1370440_comment'></div>而旧规相袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1370440_comment'></div>未甚宏丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1370440_comment'></div>檐牖东向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1370440_comment'></div>椽栾内奰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1370440_comment'></div>有祅蛊之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1370440_comment'></div>无尊严之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1370440_comment'></div>式车马者以避祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1370440_comment'></div>非以致敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1370440_comment'></div>奠蘋蘩者惟邀福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1370440_comment'></div>不惟飨德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1370440_comment'></div>犹此祀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1370440_comment'></div>不亦涹孝文于代乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1370440_comment'></div>南康其孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1370440_comment'></div>大惧夫祖德之坠于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1370440_comment'></div>因愀然而言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1370440_comment'></div>于古有召公奭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1370440_comment'></div>以区区陜服为周二伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1370440_comment'></div>行野听讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1370440_comment'></div>憩于甘棠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1370440_comment'></div>后思其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1370440_comment'></div>犹爱其树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1370440_comment'></div>其在诗曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1370440_comment'></div>勿剪勿伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1370440_comment'></div>召伯所茇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1370440_comment'></div>矧我烈祖有开国之武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1370440_comment'></div>丽天之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1370440_comment'></div>抚正万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1370440_comment'></div>照临四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1370440_comment'></div>而又储祉降德于后子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1370440_comment'></div>俾不佞起家而王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1370440_comment'></div>专城为守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1370440_comment'></div>愧不能显扬先美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1370440_comment'></div>使若黄帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1370440_comment'></div>幸君之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1370440_comment'></div>使理此土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1370440_comment'></div>敢黩于祭祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1370440_comment'></div>是亵于功烈而速其罪戾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1370440_comment'></div>一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1370440_comment'></div>因农之隙而易其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1370440_comment'></div>二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1370440_comment'></div>乘岁之丰而改其制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1370440_comment'></div>不三四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1370440_comment'></div>得请于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1370440_comment'></div>而新庙成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1370440_comment'></div>南面衮服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1370440_comment'></div>所以称尊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1370440_comment'></div>两楹阼阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1370440_comment'></div>所以定位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1370440_comment'></div>筑墉于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1370440_comment'></div>所以御侮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1370440_comment'></div>设屏于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1370440_comment'></div>所以修容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1370440_comment'></div>耽耽沈沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1370440_comment'></div>显敞靓深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1370440_comment'></div>不风而清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1370440_comment'></div>无云而阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1370440_comment'></div>前王戾止之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1370440_comment'></div>于是乎在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1370440_comment'></div>裔孙聿追之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1370440_comment'></div>于是乎举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1370440_comment'></div>不惟禁淫祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1370440_comment'></div>废非礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1370440_comment'></div>抑亦开明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1370440_comment'></div>摛耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1370440_comment'></div>欲使异日观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1370440_comment'></div>不俟请书问俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1370440_comment'></div>而知树之所由植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1370440_comment'></div>庙之所由崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1370440_comment'></div>谂于有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1370440_comment'></div>佥曰非颂声不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1370440_comment'></div>初南康之典化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1370440_comment'></div>顾尝客焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1370440_comment'></div>迨今剖符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1370440_comment'></div>则又备位于陇西公之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1370440_comment'></div>相得最旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1370440_comment'></div>见绳为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1370440_comment'></div>故敢徵成之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1370440_comment'></div>与作之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1370440_comment'></div>篆刻贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1370440_comment'></div>立于前楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1370440_comment'></div>庶拟卫悝彝鼎之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1370440_comment'></div>敢同鲁僖閟宫之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1370440_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1370440_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_169_1370440'>蔚彼白杨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1370440_comment'></div>丛生雁门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1370440_comment'></div>蒙暑翳寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1370440_comment'></div>晴天色昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1370440_comment'></div>巨抵交柯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1370440_comment'></div>龙翔虎眠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1370440_comment'></div>从古强名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1370440_comment'></div>莫知其原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1370440_comment'></div>惟昔魏帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1370440_comment'></div>于枝息鞍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1370440_comment'></div>悬垂低昂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1370440_comment'></div>厥迹犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1370440_comment'></div>大畏其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1370440_comment'></div>小怀其恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1370440_comment'></div>爰有灵祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1370440_comment'></div>号为神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1370440_comment'></div>二扉不扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1370440_comment'></div>四簋不陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1370440_comment'></div>樵苏所往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1370440_comment'></div>雉兔为邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1370440_comment'></div>于铄良牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1370440_comment'></div>时维孝孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1370440_comment'></div>下车之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1370440_comment'></div>致敬而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1370440_comment'></div>蔽芾甘棠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1370440_comment'></div>犹思其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1370440_comment'></div>绵绵葛藟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1370440_comment'></div>下庇于根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1370440_comment'></div>乃正名居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1370440_comment'></div>式崇藩垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1370440_comment'></div>山立当宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1370440_comment'></div>翼张重轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1370440_comment'></div>有赫斯皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1370440_comment'></div>既严且尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1370440_comment'></div>允矣君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1370440_comment'></div>孰如其仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1370440_comment'></div>大椿之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1370440_comment'></div>细柳之军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1370440_comment'></div>吾与元也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370366_comment'></div>今者天诛小丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370366_comment'></div>恩施群雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370366_comment'></div>岂谓偏裨。<div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370367'>右。臣得兵马使李黯状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370367_comment'></div>伏蒙圣恩赐前件物等者。伏以狂贼未平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370367_comment'></div>矜其寒苦。特颁星使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370367_comment'></div>猥降天波。衣絮八蚕之绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370367_comment'></div>暖如狐腋。弓缠九牛之角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370367_comment'></div>劲若乌号。颁及连营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370367_comment'></div>来从内府。遥知被服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370367_comment'></div>皆不惮于兵锋。缅想<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1370367", 1370367, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>操张</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370367_comment'></div>悉将穿于虏骨。欢声感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370367_comment'></div>勇气蒸腾。信山岳之可移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370367_comment'></div>岂妖氛之足灭。臣名叨将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370367_comment'></div>志埽寇雠。沐恩泽而空深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370367_comment'></div>效勤劳而尚浅。誓将忠恳以励骁雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370367_comment'></div>所守有限。不获陈谢。<div class='inline'
