id='poem_sentence_80_1370333_comment'></div>叶畅军情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1370333_comment'></div>纶言一宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1370333_comment'></div>列校相庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1370333_comment'></div>臣誓当恭承睿算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1370333_comment'></div>虔奉圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1370333_comment'></div>以安人和众为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1370333_comment'></div>用报国忘家为志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1370333_comment'></div>冀伸分寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1370333_comment'></div>上答圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1370333_comment'></div>所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1370333_comment'></div>不获陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1370333_comment'></div>臣无任感戴屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_92_1370333_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为太原郑尚书谢赐旌节等表</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370341")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370341'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370341'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370341_comment'></div>今月七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370341_comment'></div>中使尹偕至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370341_comment'></div>伏奉敕书手诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370341_comment'></div>慰喻臣及将士参佐等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370341_comment'></div>并赐臣官诰旌节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370341_comment'></div>宠命并临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370341_comment'></div>荣光謺至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370341_comment'></div>钦承捧受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370341_comment'></div>感惕难胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370341_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370341_comment'></div>臣昔为诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370341_comment'></div>所冀微禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370341_comment'></div>揣摩铅钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370341_comment'></div>际会清平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370341_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下至德配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370341_comment'></div>大明并日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370341_comment'></div>朝有多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370341_comment'></div>国无幸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370341_comment'></div>若臣庸虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370341_comment'></div>何足比数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370341_comment'></div>阶缘所职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370341_comment'></div>被服殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370341_comment'></div>居郎吏之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370341_comment'></div>巳为饕窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370341_comment'></div>立戎旃之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370341_comment'></div>安所堪任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370341_comment'></div>前奉诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370341_comment'></div>除臣节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370341_comment'></div>托肺肠而三省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370341_comment'></div>觉魂魄之九飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370341_comment'></div>恳款未申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370341_comment'></div>恩光荐及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370341_comment'></div>使从天上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370341_comment'></div>拜迎而万姓欢呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370341_comment'></div>王在日中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370341_comment'></div>照临而一方安泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370341_comment'></div>编纶言于宝轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370341_comment'></div>挥宸翰于䌽笺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370341_comment'></div>既赐诸侯之旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370341_comment'></div>又降将军之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370341_comment'></div>委之刑赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370341_comment'></div>许以便宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370341_comment'></div>臣实何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370341_comment'></div>忽蒙斯宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370341_comment'></div>重如山压。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370341_comment'></div>薰若火炎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370341_comment'></div>无以为容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370341_comment'></div>不知自处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370341_comment'></div>谨以今日准敕拜受讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370341_comment'></div>臣伏以旌惟进善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370341_comment'></div>节以诘奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370341_comment'></div>昔常传闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370341_comment'></div>今即祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370341_comment'></div>度才非将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370341_comment'></div>虽天下所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370341_comment'></div>禀令于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370341_comment'></div>岂风尘敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370341_comment'></div>誓当保安四境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370341_comment'></div>和叶三军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370341_comment'></div>洒帝泽于州闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370341_comment'></div>振皇威于边徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370341_comment'></div>难酬天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370341_comment'></div>庶竭臣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370341_comment'></div>所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1370341_comment'></div>不获陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1370341_comment'></div>无任感戴抃跃之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1370341_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　在郑儋幕府任掌书记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　在郑儋幕府，同僚可考者有严绶、齐孝若、崔能、李光进、刘胜孙五人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　在太原郑儋幕府。有文。作品：《奏太原府资望及官吏选数状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二。）</span><div id='poem_1370425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏太原府资望及官吏选数状</a><span class='authorDate'>（801年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370425")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370425_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370425'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370425'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370425_comment'></div>臣得司录参军李旦等状称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370425_comment'></div>前件府名三都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370425_comment'></div>望同两府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370425_comment'></div>吏曹近日稍易旧规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370425_comment'></div>格限之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370425_comment'></div>增加选数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370425_comment'></div>特乞奏闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370425_comment'></div>谨检开元十一年正月二十八日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370425_comment'></div>置北都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370425_comment'></div>府县资望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370425_comment'></div>并准京兆府河南府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370425_comment'></div>中閒吏曹暂有降下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370425_comment'></div>前使王缙薛兼训马燧李说并有举奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370425_comment'></div>寻蒙复旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370425_comment'></div>今准三月十五日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370425_comment'></div>停减诸州府双曹司录判司及甲曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370425_comment'></div>特蒙敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370425_comment'></div>京兆河南太原三府不在减限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370425_comment'></div>伏以太原府龙兴盛业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370425_comment'></div>天启雄藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370425_comment'></div>有义旗起建之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370425_comment'></div>为仙驾留游之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370425_comment'></div>官标留守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370425_comment'></div>驿署都亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370425_comment'></div>典章甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370425_comment'></div>制度咸在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370425_comment'></div>数年来吏部选格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370425_comment'></div>不同京兆河南两府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370425_comment'></div>官资稍下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370425_comment'></div>选数则深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370425_comment'></div>掾吏诸臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370425_comment'></div>恳有披诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370425_comment'></div>傥徇从权之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370425_comment'></div>恐乖仍旧之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370425_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈特敕吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370425_comment'></div>准元敕与京兆河南一例处分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1370425_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年8月</a>　八月，郑儋暴卒，未及安排后事，军士欲哗变，逼迫令狐楚起草遗表。楚于白刃之中操笔立成，读示三军，皆为之感泣，军情遂安。自此令狐楚声名益振。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　行军司马严绶检校工部尚书，充河东节度使。李辅光仍任监军使。令狐楚入严绶幕府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　幕府同僚可考者有李光进、李光颜兄弟，时为牙将；刘胜孙，时为节度判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　在太原严绶幕府。有文。作品：《谢敕书手诏慰问状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=802&endYear=802')">802年</a>　在太原严绶幕府，本年次子绹生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年</a>　在太原严绶幕府，与刘禹锡已有唱和往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=804&endYear=804')">804年</a>　在太原严绶幕府。正月，李景略卒于丰州，归葬秦地，途径太原，令狐楚撰文哭奠。作品：《祭丰州李大夫十八丈文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四三。）</span><div id='poem_1370443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭丰州李大夫十八丈文</a><span class='authorDate'>（804年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370443")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370443'>呜呼。龆龀之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370443_comment'></div>获见大夫。目以成器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370443_comment'></div>异于群伦。自降而迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370443_comment'></div>垂三十春。服义怀德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370443_comment'></div>远而逾亲。灵州不协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370443_comment'></div>坐谪三楚。遐服徂征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370443_comment'></div>高馆晤语。谓天之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370443_comment'></div>正直是与。捧手欲辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370443_comment'></div>以心相许。群后抗疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370443_comment'></div>讼公无辜。羽林森森。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370443_comment'></div>天授兵符。适值南还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370443_comment'></div>㯋耀神都。风天雪夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370443_comment'></div>买酒相呼。帝命并土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370443_comment'></div>喜公为副。令尹是毗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370443_comment'></div>贤王是辅。嗟我小子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370443_comment'></div>此焉婚娶。贽币既求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370443_comment'></div>酒牢亦具。河外西城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370443_comment'></div>振胡锁戎。诏迁大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370443_comment'></div>开府其中。平生相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370443_comment'></div>招我以弓。竟逼方寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370443_comment'></div>不能从公。自此违奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370443_comment'></div>无由诣谒。络绎篇章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370443_comment'></div>绸缪书札。不闻婴疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370443_comment'></div>不得留诀。仓卒一辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370443_comment'></div>寂寞长别。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370443_comment'></div>惟先将军。有庸有勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370443_comment'></div>及公嗣兴。武不害文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370443_comment'></div>义分如霜。志气干云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370443_comment'></div>头蓬面垢。报国事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370443_comment'></div>土田未封。旄钺未受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370443_comment'></div>天实福善。神明为咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370443_comment'></div>埋没黄沙。摧残白首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370443_comment'></div>虽以瞑目。岂能钳口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370443_comment'></div>孤旐翩翩。反葬秦川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370443_comment'></div>经过故府。怅望新阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370443_comment'></div>魂兮何之。音容悄然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370443_comment'></div>攀辕荐奠。苦泪潺湲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370443_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1370443_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年6月</a>　在太原严绶幕府。六月，王叔文与韦执谊渐生嫌隙。王叔文谋夺宦官兵权未成。剑南西川节度使韦皋、荆南节度使裴均、河东节度使严绶同上表，指斥王叔文等人，并请皇太子监国。叔文以母丧去位。令狐楚代严绶起草《请皇太子监国表》，《上皇太子笺》（均佚）。楚以此元和间备受宪宗恩宠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年7月</a>　七月，宦官俱文珍等屡请令皇太子监国。顺宗在内有宦官逼迫、外有方镇相次上表的情况下，乙未，诏令皇太子勾当军国政事。令狐楚代严绶起草《贺皇太子知军国表》、《贺皇太子知军国笺》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span>《贺皇太子知军国笺》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span><div id='poem_1370312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370312?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺皇太子知军国表</a><span class='authorDate'>（805年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370312")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370312_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370312'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370312'>臣得上都进奉官状报。伏承七月二十八日诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370312_comment'></div>军国政事。权令皇太子勾当者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370312_comment'></div>中贺。伏惟皇帝陛下大明御宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370312_comment'></div>至孝自天。霜露既濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370312_comment'></div>想园陵之渐近。云霞是仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370312_comment'></div>悲弓剑之方遥。内感深衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370312_comment'></div>外勉庶政。由是推赤心于俊乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370312_comment'></div>委宝历于元良。宣明两曜之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370312_comment'></div>崇重万国之本。与夫游神姑射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370312_comment'></div>义岂同风。养道大庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370312_comment'></div>礼诚异日。天下臣子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370312_comment'></div>不胜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1370312", 1370312, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>庆幸</span>。臣限以所守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370312_comment'></div>不获拜候阙庭。无任屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370312_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1370312_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺皇太子知军国笺</a><span class='authorDate'>（805年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370435")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370435'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370435'>臣某笺。伏见七月二十八日皇帝宣诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370435_comment'></div>军国政事。并权委皇太子殿下勾当者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370435_comment'></div>伏以皇帝陛下躬勤黼扆。志奉山陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370435_comment'></div>恭慕积中。殷忧发外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370435_comment'></div>瞻九庙之重。须有缵承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370435_comment'></div>以万几为烦。期在宴息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370435_comment'></div>伏惟皇太子殿下日跻睿哲。天纵钦明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370435_comment'></div>继丕业而尧历重昌。嗣鸿名而文功累盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370435_comment'></div>事有光于往古。庆实被于殊方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370435_comment'></div>率土臣心。无任欣戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370435_comment'></div>臣限以镇守。远在方隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370435_comment'></div>不获陪庆宫庭。抃舞称贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370435_comment'></div>瞻恋踊跃之至。谨奉笺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370435_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1370435_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年8月</a>　八月庚子，顺宗内禅。辛丑，改贞元二十一年为永贞元年。壬寅，贬王伾、王叔文等。乙巳，太子李纯即位，是为宪宗。令狐楚代严绶起草贺宪宗登极表。作品：《代郑尚书贺登极表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九，其中“郑尚书”当为“严绶”二表代严绶作，《文苑英华》误作“郑尚书”）</span>《为郑尚书贺登极赦表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九，其中“郑尚书”当为“严绶”二表代严绶作，《文苑英华》误作“郑尚书”）</span><div id='poem_1370309' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370309_comment'></div>臣闻天子之孝。以纂承为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370309_comment'></div>圣人之宝。以传授为公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370309_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下德合乾符。道光天宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370309_comment'></div>廓寰区以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1370309", 1370309, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>御历</span>。洒渥泽而飞龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370309_comment'></div>上以代太上之忧勤。下以副群生之欣戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370309_comment'></div>溥传天旨。大洽人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370309_comment'></div>喜气腾辉。晴云动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370309_comment'></div>黎元率舞。将校传呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370309_comment'></div>即日而万姓欢康。累旬而四海清谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370309_comment'></div>臣职当统帅。寄重方隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370309_comment'></div>庆贺之诚。倍万常品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370309_comment'></div>限以所守。不获奔赴阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370309_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1370309_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370314' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370314' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370314?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为郑尚书贺登极赦表</a><span "poem_title_1370314")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370314_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370314'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370314'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370314_comment'></div>伏奉二月二十四日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370314_comment'></div>大赦天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370314_comment'></div>霈泽自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370314_comment'></div>鸿恩匝地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370314_comment'></div>三军万姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370314_comment'></div>不胜庆跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370314_comment'></div>臣闻天地至大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370314_comment'></div>或有所不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370314_comment'></div>日月至明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370314_comment'></div>犹有所不照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370314_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下体元继统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370314_comment'></div>垂象立极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370314_comment'></div>齐轩昊之元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370314_comment'></div>冠唐虞之至仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370314_comment'></div>敷大号于天中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370314_comment'></div>揭明谟于日下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370314_comment'></div>臣以为覆载之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370314_comment'></div>大于天地矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370314_comment'></div>照临之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370314_comment'></div>明于日月矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370314_comment'></div>何则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370314_comment'></div>用刀锯而伏斧锧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370314_comment'></div>无重无轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370314_comment'></div>陛下舍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370314_comment'></div>投豺虎而御魑魅者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370314_comment'></div>无远无近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370314_comment'></div>陛下移之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370314_comment'></div>免逋逃献亩之税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370314_comment'></div>罢雕华任土之贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370314_comment'></div>出后宫之伎乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370314_comment'></div>还外国之俘囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370314_comment'></div>褒崇首先于二王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370314_comment'></div>敦叙旁周于九族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370314_comment'></div>明徵义烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370314_comment'></div>各录其裔冑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370314_comment'></div>悉数忠劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370314_comment'></div>遍增其爵级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370314_comment'></div>宣股肱之力者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370314_comment'></div>赏延于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370314_comment'></div>效爪牙之任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370314_comment'></div>赐出于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370314_comment'></div>搜沦滞之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370314_comment'></div>迁久次之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370314_comment'></div>聘士既尊于经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370314_comment'></div>问年必本于期颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370314_comment'></div>在幽隐而不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370314_comment'></div>虽细微而皆及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370314_comment'></div>欢声雷动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370314_comment'></div>喜气云腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370314_comment'></div>百姓知圣人之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370314_comment'></div>万物睹圣人之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370314_comment'></div>普天率土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370314_comment'></div>无不庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370314_comment'></div>臣叨居藩服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370314_comment'></div>累沐恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370314_comment'></div>抃舞欣欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370314_comment'></div>倍百恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370314_comment'></div>所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370314_comment'></div>不获称庆阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370314_comment'></div>臣及将士官吏百姓等无任踊跃屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1370314_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年8月</a>　在太原严绶幕府。有文。作品：《为郑尚书贺册皇太子状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四二，其中“郑尚书”当为“严绶”按，郑儋镇河东时，无策皇太子事，实为代严绶作。）</span>《贺册太子赦表》<span href='/Writing/1370394?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为郑尚书贺册皇太子状</a><span class='authorDate'>（805年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370394")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370394_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370394'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370394'>臣闻于宣政殿册皇太子讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370394_comment'></div>伏以建崇储位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370394_comment'></div>光启春闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370394_comment'></div>万方以贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370394_comment'></div>九服同庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370394_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下诞敷圣训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370394_comment'></div>光启天慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370394_comment'></div>咸元贞于国经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370394_comment'></div>钟福庆于邦本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370394_comment'></div>皇太子温恭表德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370394_comment'></div>仁孝因心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370394_comment'></div>方毓质于龙楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370394_comment'></div>肇增辉于望苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370394_comment'></div>臣戎守有限。<div class='inline' showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺册太子赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（805年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370315")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370315'>臣某言。伏奉今月九日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370315_comment'></div>皇太子册礼云覃恩与万方同其惠泽者。国庆遐宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370315_comment'></div>天波曲被。怀生之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370315_comment'></div>咸共欣荣。中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370315_comment'></div>臣闻德教所加。一人有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370315_comment'></div>元良既立。万国以贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370315_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下至化旁流。神功广运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370315_comment'></div>以为义莫重于主鬯。礼无大于承祧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370315_comment'></div>考古扬前星之光。顺人宏少海之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370315_comment'></div>诞敷明诏。宣告庶方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370315_comment'></div>雷初动于地中。风已行于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370315_comment'></div>由是哀矜罪戾。甄奖功勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370315_comment'></div>表顺孙孝子之门。秩名山大川之祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370315_comment'></div>仁无不覆。惠无不均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370315_comment'></div>草木惟繇。鸟兽咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370315_comment'></div>率土臣子。不胜庆抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370315_comment'></div>臣限守藩镇。不获陪位阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370315_comment'></div>踊跃称庆。无任屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370315_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1370315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年9月</a>　九月，刘禹锡、程异等坐王叔文党，贬远州刺史。十一月，贬韦执谊为崖州司马，刘禹锡等再贬远州司马，是为“八司马”事件，令狐楚担心受牵累，本年后与刘禹锡中断往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年10月18日</a>　在太原严绶幕府。孟冬月十有八日，有文。作品：《沁源县琴高灵泉碑记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四三。）</span><div id='poem_1370439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁源县琴高灵泉碑记</a><span class='authorDate'>（805年10月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370439")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370439'>仙人琴高。生于周而游于冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370439_comment'></div>尝入砀水。沈而不濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370439_comment'></div>时乘赤鲤。周旋自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370439_comment'></div>河东冀州之城也。前此尝命有司庙于沁水之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370439_comment'></div>有冽寒泉。在堂之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370439_comment'></div>广圜累步。澄湛盈尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370439_comment'></div>嘻。灵踪汗漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370439_comment'></div>虽羽化于何乡。而真理希夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370439_comment'></div>或鳞潜于此地。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370439_comment'></div>则何以旱暵而不耗。霖霪而不盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370439_comment'></div>居人乞灵以赴愬。游子玩奇而濯弄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370439_comment'></div>澹乎不知其几百年也。贞元十五祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370439_comment'></div>郡守之子弟。敢以荤血馔于傍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370439_comment'></div>腥膻既漫。清泚遂涸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370439_comment'></div>似有扃闭。孰知根源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370439_comment'></div>迨兹七稔。无复一勺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370439_comment'></div>永贞之元年。观察使尚书右仆射冯翊严公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370439_comment'></div>以清静□其心。以中和乐其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370439_comment'></div>申命前清源令范阳卢惮假符于州。逾月而吏知耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370439_comment'></div>逾时而人知敬。一年而生物尽康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370439_comment'></div>众绩其凝。由是抗怀仙风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370439_comment'></div>注意灵泉。且曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370439_comment'></div>刺山而飞者。传于故志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370439_comment'></div>闻绮而赴者。载在前言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370439_comment'></div>吾其祷焉。傥可复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370439_comment'></div>秋九月一日。率其属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370439_comment'></div>有摄长史程义光。摄司马周利用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370439_comment'></div>军从事王僔州。主簿赵鄂王青溪杨果云连道冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370439_comment'></div>并军吏群从数十人。致斋陈信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370439_comment'></div>肸蚃如答。初以神视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370439_comment'></div>厌浥而未融。徐以气听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370439_comment'></div>湔准而始达。奠未彻而可以鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370439_comment'></div>晷不移而可以汲。其明日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370439_comment'></div>潏然有响。澄然无波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370439_comment'></div>旧痕皆平。故味不爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370439_comment'></div>州闾喜骇。瞻观奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370439_comment'></div>乞以其状献于府朝。而卢君善无近名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370439_comment'></div>嫌不语怪。将使感通神速之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370439_comment'></div>寂寥无声。越十月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370439_comment'></div>楚闻风异之。伐石为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370439_comment'></div>呜呼。圣人之所以观象设教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370439_comment'></div>神而化之者。无他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370439_comment'></div>其要在于祸淫福谦。惩恶劝善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370439_comment'></div>苟或淫昧。将焉训斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370439_comment'></div>吾知卢君之洗心餐和。勤力抱素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370439_comment'></div>前领辽山也。未及周岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370439_comment'></div>获白鹿以归。聿来沁源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370439_comment'></div>斋沐于赤松观。有四白鹤自天翔集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370439_comment'></div>是故精意专感。急于置邮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370439_comment'></div>灵钓而元关洞开。神驱而幽键迎解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370439_comment'></div>有以知神明之与仁助。信盖章乎州民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370439_comment'></div>于是洁其涯隒。新其庙貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370439_comment'></div>入于门者。不俟约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370439_comment'></div>自然斋庄。如承水仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370439_comment'></div>若睹龙鲤。上可以列瑞典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370439_comment'></div>下可以编幽经。目为灵泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370439_comment'></div>盖传信也。时永贞元年孟冬月十有八日记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370439_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1370439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_1370329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370329'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370329'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370329_comment'></div>伏见制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370329_comment'></div>大行皇帝灵驾剋以某月日迁座崇陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370329_comment'></div>先太后梓宫自靖陵启发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370329_comment'></div>同时合祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370329_comment'></div>万邦永慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370329_comment'></div>攀奉山园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370329_comment'></div>圣情难处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370329_comment'></div>中慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370329_comment'></div>先朝临御悠长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370329_comment'></div>威灵遐被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370329_comment'></div>储祉传圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370329_comment'></div>以福四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370329_comment'></div>今祇祔礼终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370329_comment'></div>清庙如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370329_comment'></div>率土臣庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370329_comment'></div>实谓哀荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370329_comment'></div>臣职忝方隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370329_comment'></div>分忧地远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370329_comment'></div>不获仰陪下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370329_comment'></div>奉慰外朝。<div showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元日进马并鞍辔状</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370402")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370402'>右。臣伏以元日开岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370402_comment'></div>东风发春。人神大和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370402_comment'></div>天地交泰。伏惟皇帝陛下鸿猷更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370402_comment'></div>宝祚惟新。协三朝之会同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370402_comment'></div>受万国之归庆。臣某职当分阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370402_comment'></div>属忝维城。未耸翼于丹霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370402_comment'></div>空驰心于皇极。前件马并鞍辔等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370402_comment'></div>驰驱有度。雕镂初成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370402_comment'></div>愿将行地之功。以奉如山之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370402_comment'></div>干烦宸严。伏增战汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370402_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1370402_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153572' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153572' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153572?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郑尚书贺册皇太后表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1153572")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153572_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153572'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153572'>臣某言。臣伏奉五月二十八日敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153572_comment'></div>尊太上皇后。恩覃日下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153572_comment'></div>欢动天中。臣伏以皇太后坤德合符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153572_comment'></div>阴灵表庆。化光宫职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153572_comment'></div>道赞国风。伏惟皇帝仁圣宅心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153572_comment'></div>文明恭巳。遵承孝理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153572_comment'></div>严奉慈颜。献<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1153572", 1153572, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>宝绶</span>于内朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153572_comment'></div>宣玉册于中禁。彰明顺德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153572_comment'></div>知陛下就养之勤。表正母仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153572_comment'></div>见陛下归安之盛。万国所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153572_comment'></div>四方是刑。人臣之恳愿既申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153572_comment'></div>品物之欢心斯洽。臣叨承寄任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153572_comment'></div>限守藩隅。不及陪位阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153572_comment'></div>抃舞称贺。无任耸庆踊悦之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153572_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1153572_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370319' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370319' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370319?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑尚书贺册太后礼毕赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370319")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370319_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370319'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370319'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370319_comment'></div>伏奉五月二十八日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370319_comment'></div>皇太后光膺茂典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370319_comment'></div>诞受鸿猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370319_comment'></div>恩荣庆锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370319_comment'></div>覃被率土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370319_comment'></div>中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370319_comment'></div>臣闻天子以德教而兆人庆赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370319_comment'></div>明王以孝理而百神和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370319_comment'></div>伏以皇太后秉德阴凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370319_comment'></div>体仁坤厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370319_comment'></div>宏是内则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370319_comment'></div>顺于先朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370319_comment'></div>道配轩皇之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370319_comment'></div>功参文母之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370319_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下孝承丕绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370319_comment'></div>仁嗣宝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370319_comment'></div>则天之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370319_comment'></div>事地以察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370319_comment'></div>昭彰慈训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370319_comment'></div>光启尊名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370319_comment'></div>发德音于上元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370319_comment'></div>流惠泽于下土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370319_comment'></div>陷疏网者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370319_comment'></div>许其减等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370319_comment'></div>养高堂者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370319_comment'></div>锡以加封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370319_comment'></div>粟帛遍沾于耆年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370319_comment'></div>门闾必表于仁里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370319_comment'></div>悉使怀生庶类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370319_comment'></div>行道群心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370319_comment'></div>非独各亲其所亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370319_comment'></div>无不长人之所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370319_comment'></div>湛恩布濩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370319_comment'></div>盛礼丰融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370319_comment'></div>信可通神明而光四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370319_comment'></div>天下臣子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370319_comment'></div>不胜庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370319_comment'></div>臣限于镇守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370319_comment'></div>远在方隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370319_comment'></div>不获躬诣阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370319_comment'></div>抃舞称庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370319_comment'></div>无任耸踊庆幸之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1370319_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370331' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370331' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370331?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺顺宗谥议表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370331")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370331_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370331'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370331'>臣某言。伏奉六月十四日敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370331_comment'></div>太常奏大行太皇尊谥曰至德大圣安孝皇帝。庙号曰顺宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370331_comment'></div>臣某诚感诚庆顿首顿首。臣闻入庙观德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370331_comment'></div>载在前言。闻谥知行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370331_comment'></div>传于故志。伏惟顺宗大圣安孝皇帝统承九圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370331_comment'></div>保乂万邦。继耀大明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370331_comment'></div>合符真宰。方同天以下覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370331_comment'></div>俄厌代以上仙。伏惟皇帝陛下哀慕未忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370331_comment'></div>孝思罔极。痛衣冠之永閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370331_comment'></div>攀弓剑而无阶。殷荐鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370331_comment'></div>光昭懿德。庙号非徵于汉魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370331_comment'></div>帝图自掩于羲轩。百代见圣人之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370331_comment'></div>四方知君子之孝。率土臣子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370331_comment'></div>以欣以感。臣限于镇守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370331_comment'></div>远在方隅。不获奔赴阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370331_comment'></div>陪位称贺。无任踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370331_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1370331_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370328' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370328' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370328?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉慰过山陵表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370328")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370328_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370328'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370328'>伏承顺宗至德大圣大安孝皇帝奄过山陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370328_comment'></div>率土臣庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370328_comment'></div>不胜号慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370328_comment'></div>伏惟陛下孝思天至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370328_comment'></div>祗事荐诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370328_comment'></div>精贯昊穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370328_comment'></div>礼备园寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370328_comment'></div>攀号罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370328_comment'></div>圣情难居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370328_comment'></div>臣谬列藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370328_comment'></div>限于守职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370328_comment'></div>不获奔走陪慰内庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370328_comment'></div>无任感惕兢越之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1370328_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>　仍在严绶幕府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　正月尚在严绶幕府。作品：《贺赦表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span><div id='poem_1370313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370313?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370313")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370313'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370313'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370313_comment'></div>臣伏奉今月十一日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370313_comment'></div>元德融明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370313_comment'></div>声闻于宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370313_comment'></div>鸿名光大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370313_comment'></div>充塞于乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370313_comment'></div>与物皆春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370313_comment'></div>大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370313_comment'></div>臣当时宣流渥泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370313_comment'></div>腾布耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370313_comment'></div>恩均而万物昭苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370313_comment'></div>庆洽而三军鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370313_comment'></div>中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370313_comment'></div>臣闻覆载无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370313_comment'></div>天地所以为大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370313_comment'></div>照临不巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370313_comment'></div>日月所以为大明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370313_comment'></div>六位因时以成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370313_comment'></div>一代观象而设教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370313_comment'></div>肇自古昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370313_comment'></div>垂为宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370313_comment'></div>伏惟睿圣文武皇帝陛下并日而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370313_comment'></div>配天为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370313_comment'></div>冠三皇之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370313_comment'></div>宏十圣之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370313_comment'></div>保合太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370313_comment'></div>缉熙帝载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370313_comment'></div>是以廓清氛雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370313_comment'></div>曾不累旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370313_comment'></div>虔奉郊禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370313_comment'></div>未尝虚岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370313_comment'></div>百蛮梯航以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1370313", 1370313, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>内面</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370313_comment'></div>万国歌舞而宅心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370313_comment'></div>所谓巍乎其有成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370313_comment'></div>焕乎其有文章也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370313_comment'></div>尚复劳谦仄席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370313_comment'></div>勤恤纳隍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370313_comment'></div>释累系之幽囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370313_comment'></div>无分轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370313_comment'></div>归遐远之放逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370313_comment'></div>不问存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370313_comment'></div>弃逋债于穷人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370313_comment'></div>戒多求于贪吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370313_comment'></div>悯朔边之介士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370313_comment'></div>厚其寒衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370313_comment'></div>恢武功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370313_comment'></div>褒阙里之冑嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370313_comment'></div>贲以布帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370313_comment'></div>振文教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370313_comment'></div>推恩而九族既睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370313_comment'></div>行庆而六师用张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370313_comment'></div>忠贞必表于门闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370313_comment'></div>耆耋遍羞其牢醴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370313_comment'></div>百神咸秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370313_comment'></div>一物不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370313_comment'></div>安人之所未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370313_comment'></div>理人之所未理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370313_comment'></div>天波涣汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370313_comment'></div>纶旨丁宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370313_comment'></div>有以知天地覆载之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370313_comment'></div>有以见日月照临之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370313_comment'></div>天下臣妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370313_comment'></div>不胜庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370313_comment'></div>臣限守藩镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370313_comment'></div>不获称庆阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1370313_comment'></div>无任抃跃欣贺之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1370313_comment'></div>谨遣某官奉表陈贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1370313_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　稍后迁节度判官，加检校监察御史职。迁节度判官后，缀集在桂、并四府任掌书记期间所撰的一百九十三篇表奏，编为《白云孺子表奏集》十卷。<br /><a href="javascript: href='/Writing/1370389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐毯价绢状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370389")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370389'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370389_comment'></div>监军使李辅光回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370389_comment'></div>奉宣恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370389_comment'></div>赐臣前件绢者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370389_comment'></div>臣当道比年未丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370389_comment'></div>经费不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370389_comment'></div>惧乏供亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370389_comment'></div>惭无智能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370389_comment'></div>陛下散烛幽之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370389_comment'></div>垂逮下之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370389_comment'></div>丝纶既出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370389_comment'></div>缣帛贲来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370389_comment'></div>数至累千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370389_comment'></div>价盈巨万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370389_comment'></div>广狭中量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370389_comment'></div>鲜明如冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370389_comment'></div>足以赡三军之赐予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370389_comment'></div>充百工之饩廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370389_comment'></div>捧受欣抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370389_comment'></div>不知所裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370389_comment'></div>无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1370389_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370321' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370321' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370321?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺白鹿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370321")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370321_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370321'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370321'>臣某言。臣得进奏院状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370321_comment'></div>中书门下奏贺。于醴泉县建陵柏城获白鹿一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370321_comment'></div>圣敬日跻。休祥荐至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370321_comment'></div>臣某谨按孝经援神契曰。王者德至禽兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370321_comment'></div>则白鹿见。伏惟陛下盛德配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370321_comment'></div>深仁育物。和气交感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370321_comment'></div>出为休徵。懿此异兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370321_comment'></div>挺兹奇表。在峤山之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370321_comment'></div>宛是随仙。来魏阙之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370321_comment'></div>如将率舞。天下称述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370321_comment'></div>兆人欢庆。昔者周因征伐而获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370321_comment'></div>汉自祭祀而臻。比今无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370321_comment'></div>宜有惭德。臣某幸逢昭代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370321_comment'></div>获睹元功。欣抃之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370321_comment'></div>倍百恒品。所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370321_comment'></div>不获随例称庆阙庭。无任屏营踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370321_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1370321_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人作谢防秋回赐将士等物状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370365")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370365'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370365'>右件将士。中使朱孝诚监领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370365_comment'></div>某月日平安到太原。其赏物并敕给付讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370365_comment'></div>臣伏以受命以行。人臣之节斯著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370365_comment'></div>及期而代。君父之仁已深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370365_comment'></div>陛下爱育武夫。绥怀猛士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370365_comment'></div>采薇遣戍。既霈挟纩之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370365_comment'></div>出车劳旋。又有分缣之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370365_comment'></div>才识家而兢入。俄拜赐以嵩呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370365_comment'></div>尽忘征役之劳。固感生成之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370365_comment'></div>况臣叨居将帅。获沐恩波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370365_comment'></div>所守有限。不获陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370365_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1370365_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370368?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人谢赐天德防秋将士絁绢状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370368")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370368'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370368'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370368_comment'></div>臣今月七日中使朱孝诚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370368_comment'></div>伏奉诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370368_comment'></div>兼宣恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370368_comment'></div>赐前件絁绢等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370368_comment'></div>臣伏以武夫之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370368_comment'></div>职在防虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370368_comment'></div>壮士之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370368_comment'></div>乐从征役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370368_comment'></div>陛下仁慈广被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370368_comment'></div>渥泽旁流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370368_comment'></div>谕以功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370368_comment'></div>赐之绵帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370368_comment'></div>荷殊私而东拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370368_comment'></div>悉有兼衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370368_comment'></div>贾馀勇而西行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370368_comment'></div>若无远道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370368_comment'></div>同将日力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370368_comment'></div>共振天声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370368_comment'></div>臣猥守藩隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370368_comment'></div>叨居将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370368_comment'></div>欣荣感戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370368_comment'></div>实百恒情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1370368_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370369' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370369' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370369?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人谢赐将军官告状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370369")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370369_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370369'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370369'>右。臣中使朱孝诚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370369_comment'></div>伏奉诏命慰问臣。并宣慰旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370369_comment'></div>允臣所奏。当使诸将官赐前件告身者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370369_comment'></div>宠命从天。荣光溢路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370369_comment'></div>欢呼感戴。皆不自胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370369_comment'></div>臣素质懦愚。叨居上将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370369_comment'></div>微诚空竭。薄效未伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370369_comment'></div>伏蒙陛下曲降天波。俯加王泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370369_comment'></div>华资清秩。周及于百夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370369_comment'></div>喜气欢声。喧传于一道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370369_comment'></div>家藏宝轴。人受纶言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370369_comment'></div>三军惊非次之荣。万井贺殊情之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370369_comment'></div>誓将苦节。上答明恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370369_comment'></div>谨准敕捧受分给讫。臣与诸将等限以所守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370369_comment'></div>不获诣阙陈谢。无任抃跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370369_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1370369_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭侄女行军夫人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370444")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370444'>年月日。某官某致祭于故十三侄女行军夫人之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370444_comment'></div>呜呼。妇德尚柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370444_comment'></div>以宜其家。人之不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370444_comment'></div>生也有涯。侧闻夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370444_comment'></div>明懿秾华。辉夺夜光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370444_comment'></div>鲜侔晨葩。行军之妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370444_comment'></div>尚书之女。动而中礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370444_comment'></div>欲不踰矩。婉彼宋子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370444_comment'></div>归于郑武。主吏之昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370444_comment'></div>副军大卤。云霄兹始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370444_comment'></div>琴瑟方调。孰云大年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370444_comment'></div>曾莫崇朝。煜煜蕣华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370444_comment'></div>不思风飘。瀼瀼薤露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370444_comment'></div>先旦而消。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370444_comment'></div>昔也北来。绣帷亏蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370444_comment'></div>今兹南去。丹旐容曳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370444_comment'></div>逝矣冥漠。宛然慈惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370444_comment'></div>嫡女坠心。良人迸涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370444_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。本支百世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370444_comment'></div>如水一源。况是鳏夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370444_comment'></div>弥怜小孙。千龄共尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370444_comment'></div>万化如存。申奠致词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370444_comment'></div>悲何可言。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370444_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1370444_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370392' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370392' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370392?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为五台山僧谢赐袈裟等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370392")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370392_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370392'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370392'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370392_comment'></div>中使苏明俊至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370392_comment'></div>奉宣圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370392_comment'></div>赐臣巾袜香茶念珠袈裟等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370392_comment'></div>伏以推恩之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370392_comment'></div>法雨露而必均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370392_comment'></div>受施之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370392_comment'></div>戴邱山而不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370392_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下为人心印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370392_comment'></div>得佛髻珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370392_comment'></div>垂衣于空寂之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370392_comment'></div>倒屣于清凉之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370392_comment'></div>每因令月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370392_comment'></div>常降信臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370392_comment'></div>辇珍宝于九天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370392_comment'></div>散芳馨于十地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370392_comment'></div>巾裁吴纻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370392_comment'></div>靡不轻盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370392_comment'></div>帔衲齐纨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370392_comment'></div>无非丽密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370392_comment'></div>臣某等名非长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370392_comment'></div>迹在凡夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370392_comment'></div>既结袜以经行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370392_comment'></div>又焚香而宴坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370392_comment'></div>啜楚山之新茗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370392_comment'></div>烦恼顿除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370392_comment'></div>持越海之名珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370392_comment'></div>圣贤可数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370392_comment'></div>而煎和百品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370392_comment'></div>周遍万僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370392_comment'></div>睹奕叶以重光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370392_comment'></div>知分畦而謺庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370392_comment'></div>岂大雄慈悲之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370392_comment'></div>尽上帝福德之田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370392_comment'></div>誓当洁已祷天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370392_comment'></div>虔诚报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370392_comment'></div>以无疆为圣寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370392_comment'></div>以常乐为昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370392_comment'></div>长承覆护之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370392_comment'></div>永助清平之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370392_comment'></div>限以修习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370392_comment'></div>不获匍匐陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370392_comment'></div>无任感戴之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1370392_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢口敕慰问状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370372")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370372'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370372'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370372_comment'></div>中使孟升进至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370372_comment'></div>伏奉口敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370372_comment'></div>慰问臣及将士等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370372_comment'></div>臣素非公才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370372_comment'></div>叨总戎律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370372_comment'></div>清平无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370372_comment'></div>绩用未彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370372_comment'></div>伏惟陛下子惠兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370372_comment'></div>天成万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370372_comment'></div>降星分之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370372_comment'></div>宣纶出之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370372_comment'></div>问以炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370372_comment'></div>勉其劳役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370372_comment'></div>恩踰素望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370372_comment'></div>荣冠常伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370372_comment'></div>跪听欢呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370372_comment'></div>众心如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370372_comment'></div>臣等不胜感戴之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1370372_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端午进鞍马等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370404")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370404'>右。臣伏以五者天之成数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370404_comment'></div>夏者天之仁时。伏以陛下用仁时而长养群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370404_comment'></div>举成数而陶甄品物。是以百蛮委瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370404_comment'></div>万国归诚。同瞻日月之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370404_comment'></div>共奉乾坤之寿。臣方从边役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370404_comment'></div>未在周行。谬宣力于清朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370404_comment'></div>窃驰心于令节。前件马等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370404_comment'></div>柔驯既久。雕饰初成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370404_comment'></div>敢因五日之良。以续千年之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370404_comment'></div>千冒陈献。伏用兢惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370404_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1370404_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又进银器物并行鞋等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370407")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370407'>右。伏以月维正阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370407_comment'></div>日次南午。千官拜称觞之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370407_comment'></div>万国陈执圭之礼。将以嗣续圣寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370407_comment'></div>延洪昌期。盖朝廷之旧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370407_comment'></div>乃臣子之常事。前件银器等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370407_comment'></div>或便于用。正当其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370407_comment'></div>惭经万里之遥。愿献九天之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370407_comment'></div>尘黩宸鉴。无任战惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370407_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1370407_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人谢赐口脂等并历日状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370381")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370381'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370381'>右。中使吴千金至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370381_comment'></div>伏奉敕书慰问臣。并赐前件口脂腊脂红雪紫雪各一合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370381_comment'></div>并历日一卷等者。伏以岁将更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370381_comment'></div>节及嘉平。陛下凝香为膏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370381_comment'></div>聚药成散。颁日月于历上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370381_comment'></div>奋龙鸾于笔端。星分九天之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370381_comment'></div>云布一日之泽。此诚无私之殊造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370381_comment'></div>均养之深仁。而臣空抱愚忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370381_comment'></div>曾无方略。一居藩镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370381_comment'></div>三度受恩。朱奁忽开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370381_comment'></div>鲜腻与芳馨相杂。素编既列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370381_comment'></div>闰馀将分至不差。披寻而齿算延长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370381_comment'></div>涂傅而口容芳润。油云之覆逾广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370381_comment'></div>无以胜任。绵地之封粗安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370381_comment'></div>未为报效。捧受赏玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370381_comment'></div>形神涣然。无任感戴之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370381_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1370381_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人谢端午赐物等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370380")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370380'>右。中使王进卿至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370380_comment'></div>伏奉诏书慰问臣。兼宣恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370380_comment'></div>赐臣及诸将衣并百索银器等者。臣伏以夏之为仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370380_comment'></div>实由乎长养。王者所宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370380_comment'></div>莫重于贤能。故事将锡长年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370380_comment'></div>皆于今月。因颁珍玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370380_comment'></div>遐及庶方。诚上帝之殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370380_comment'></div>信天朝之盛典。臣才无所取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370380_comment'></div>政不足称。获守司存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370380_comment'></div>已为尸忝。岂意九天之庆赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370380_comment'></div>每岁必来。五日之祺祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370380_comment'></div>无年不受。衣裳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1370380", 1370380, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>雾叠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370380_comment'></div>诏旨云繁。箧中盈䌽丝之索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370380_comment'></div>案上满真金之器。方圆通用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370380_comment'></div>红紫交光。命轻而服拜难胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370380_comment'></div>身贱而铺尘不称。以荣为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370380_comment'></div>当喜而忧。终无补于成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370380_comment'></div>空有惭于僭赏。并准敕捧受兼分给诸将讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370380_comment'></div>所守有限。不获陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370380_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1370380_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370384?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐春衣牙尺状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370384")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370384'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370384'>右。中使某至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370384_comment'></div>伏奉诏书。宣赐前件物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370384_comment'></div>臣伏以衣服者身之文章。尺寸者王之律度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370384_comment'></div>被于四体。不衷则灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370384_comment'></div>考以二分。无差为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370384_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下陶蒸万类。轨物兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370384_comment'></div>每及新春。皆颁上赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370384_comment'></div>其或才堪国用。智代天工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370384_comment'></div>福至而惊。名成犹惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370384_comment'></div>循省涯分。比数艺能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370384_comment'></div>臣实无任。累承斯宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370384_comment'></div>曳紫光于腰下。称佩黄金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370384_comment'></div>操素质于掌中。如持白璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370384_comment'></div>窥看耀日。举止生风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370384_comment'></div>诚圣主全覆育之仁。顾微臣无秉持之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370384_comment'></div>蒙恩过厚。忍愧逾深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370384_comment'></div>终申一寸之功。用答九重之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370384_comment'></div>欣荣感惕。不胜自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370384_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1370384_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370385' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370385' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370385?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370385")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370385_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370385'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370385'>右。中使骆元荣至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370385_comment'></div>伏奉敕书手诏。慰问臣等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370385_comment'></div>并赐臣春衣二副。牙尺一枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370385_comment'></div>军将衣二十副者。臣伏以行庆于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370385_comment'></div>惟德所广。受赏于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370385_comment'></div>无功则难。臣实何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370385_comment'></div>叨居重任。履冰非惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370385_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1370385", 1370385, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>食檗</span>为甘。今者伏蒙陛下推汉后解衣之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370385_comment'></div>宠锡春服。稽有虞审度之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370385_comment'></div>荣颁象尺。乐官考正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370385_comment'></div>无累黍之差。女御裁缝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370385_comment'></div>有夺朱之丽。而况端平皎洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370385_comment'></div>无惭七宝。轻盈綷䌨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370385_comment'></div>不谢六铢。此臣所以捧观而似睹钧衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370385_comment'></div>服拜而如生羽翼。谨便分散诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370385_comment'></div>传示众人。感戴欣抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370385_comment'></div>欢与臣同。所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370385_comment'></div>不获拜谢。无任欣跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370385_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1370385_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏百姓王士昊割股状</a><span
