"poem_title_1370430")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370430'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370430'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370430_comment'></div>臣得太原府牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370430_comment'></div>前件人为母阿张患病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370430_comment'></div>割股奉母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370430_comment'></div>其母所得疾渐损者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370430_comment'></div>臣伏以登于大孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370430_comment'></div>在礼为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370430_comment'></div>忍其甚痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370430_comment'></div>于人不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370430_comment'></div>王士昊长于市井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370430_comment'></div>利在锥刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370430_comment'></div>誓以诚明之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370430_comment'></div>疗其羸老之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370430_comment'></div>割肉于股。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370430_comment'></div>馈羹于堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370430_comment'></div>信可以感通神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370430_comment'></div>风变人俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370430_comment'></div>某猥司廉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370430_comment'></div>获守方隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370430_comment'></div>以此至性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370430_comment'></div>恐须旌表。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1370430_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370431' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370431' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370431?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏榆次县冯秀诚割股奉母状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370431")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370431_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370431'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370431'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370431_comment'></div>臣得太原府牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370431_comment'></div>前件人为母久患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370431_comment'></div>割股奉母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370431_comment'></div>所疾渐损者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370431_comment'></div>臣差当县主簿刘戡检验得状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370431_comment'></div>具如前申者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370431_comment'></div>臣伏以纵螫及肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370431_comment'></div>口犹难忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370431_comment'></div>援刀刺骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370431_comment'></div>心岂易安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370431_comment'></div>前件人出于畎亩之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370431_comment'></div>长在草茅之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370431_comment'></div>天生仁孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370431_comment'></div>日用元和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370431_comment'></div>忘甚痛于已躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370431_comment'></div>期有瘳于亲疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370431_comment'></div>人伦共感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370431_comment'></div>名教所宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370431_comment'></div>斯实陛下仁奄周王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370431_comment'></div>孝逾虞帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370431_comment'></div>陶蒸动物之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370431_comment'></div>启迪仁人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370431_comment'></div>况臣守在方隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370431_comment'></div>职司廉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370431_comment'></div>据其至行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370431_comment'></div>恐合褒称。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1370431_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢宣慰诸州军镇等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370375")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370375'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370375'>右。中使至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370375_comment'></div>伏奉某月日诏书。令中使宣慰诸州刺史外镇将士等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370375_comment'></div>令臣亦使人安抚者。臣准诏差虞候张液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370375_comment'></div>随中使某所在存问。以某月日却到太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370375_comment'></div>伏以设官分职。邦国之恒规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370375_comment'></div>秉义纳忠。人臣之素分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370375_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下嘉其奉上。念以守边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370375_comment'></div>降驿骑于九重。谕天心于万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370375_comment'></div>法南风之长养。岂择卑微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370375_comment'></div>并白日之照临。不遗遐远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370375_comment'></div>边城将校。井里黎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370375_comment'></div>竞鼓舞于皇明。尽沾濡于圣泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370375_comment'></div>室家相庆。关塞无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370375_comment'></div>臣忝守戎旃。无任忻抃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370375_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1370375_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进异马驹表</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370356")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370356'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370356_comment'></div>得当道征马使穆林状称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370356_comment'></div>忻州定襄县王进封村界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370356_comment'></div>去五月十二日夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370356_comment'></div>孳化马群内异驹一匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370356_comment'></div>白騧文马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370356_comment'></div>画图送到者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370356_comment'></div>臣谨差虞候辛峻专往考验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370356_comment'></div>并母取到太原府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370356_comment'></div>而毛色变换与青騧色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370356_comment'></div>驼头跌额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370356_comment'></div>红鼻肉骏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370356_comment'></div>尾上茸毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370356_comment'></div>额带星及旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370356_comment'></div>肋骨左右各十八枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370356_comment'></div>四蹄青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370356_comment'></div>两眼黑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370356_comment'></div>续得穆林状称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370356_comment'></div>当生之夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370356_comment'></div>群马皆嘶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370356_comment'></div>灵质炳然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370356_comment'></div>休徵备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370356_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370356_comment'></div>臣闻马之精也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370356_comment'></div>自天而降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370356_comment'></div>马之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370356_comment'></div>行地无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370356_comment'></div>是以武藉其威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370356_comment'></div>文荣其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370356_comment'></div>谨按马经云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370356_comment'></div>肋数十六者行千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370356_comment'></div>伏惟陛下握负图之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370356_comment'></div>总服皂之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370356_comment'></div>异物殊祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370356_comment'></div>蔚然丛集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370356_comment'></div>臣观前件驹灵表挺特。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370356_comment'></div>雄姿逸异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370356_comment'></div>颈昂昂而凤顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370356_comment'></div>尾宛宛以虬蟠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370356_comment'></div>信坤元之利贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370356_comment'></div>诚太乙之元贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370356_comment'></div>自将到府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370356_comment'></div>便丽于宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370356_comment'></div>每饮以清池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370356_comment'></div>牧于芳草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370356_comment'></div>则弥日翘立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370356_comment'></div>驱之不前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370356_comment'></div>及长风时来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370356_comment'></div>微雨新霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370356_comment'></div>辄骧首奔骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370356_comment'></div>追之莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370356_comment'></div>臣某恒亲省视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370356_comment'></div>专遣柔驯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370356_comment'></div>倘骏骨峰生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370356_comment'></div>奇毛日就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370356_comment'></div>获登华厩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370356_comment'></div>既备属车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370356_comment'></div>远齐飞兔之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370356_comment'></div>上奉应龙之驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370356_comment'></div>天下大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370356_comment'></div>微臣至愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370356_comment'></div>见今养饲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370356_comment'></div>至秋中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370356_comment'></div>即专进献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370356_comment'></div>伏惟陛下兼爱好奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1370356_comment'></div>想其风彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1370356_comment'></div>今谨图画随表上进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1370356_comment'></div>伏乞圣恩宣付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1370356_comment'></div>俾此丕烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1370356_comment'></div>垂于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1370356_comment'></div>臣无任战越之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1370356_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进异马驹状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370421")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370421'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370421_comment'></div>臣得征马使穆材状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370421_comment'></div>谨具毛色如前者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370421_comment'></div>臣伏以行地之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370421_comment'></div>莫神于马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370421_comment'></div>擅华名者则众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370421_comment'></div>效奇质者甚稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370421_comment'></div>伏惟陛下广大际天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370421_comment'></div>高明配日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370421_comment'></div>殊祥竞发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370421_comment'></div>休祉荐臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370421_comment'></div>前件马禀天驷之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370421_comment'></div>体坤元之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370421_comment'></div>毛拳惟细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370421_comment'></div>鬣赤而高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370421_comment'></div>尾掉肉而蜿蟺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370421_comment'></div>额带星而倜傥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370421_comment'></div>臣谨差虞候辛峻专往覆视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370421_comment'></div>俱如前列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370421_comment'></div>峻云双瞳有耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370421_comment'></div>四蹄如削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370421_comment'></div>宛然天产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370421_comment'></div>定是龙媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370421_comment'></div>允协建午之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370421_comment'></div>光昭太乙之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370421_comment'></div>臣见今就太原府养调旬月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370421_comment'></div>稍任行步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370421_comment'></div>即专陈献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370421_comment'></div>谨差某官闻奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1370421_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐僧尼告身并华严院额状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370391")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370391'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370391'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370391_comment'></div>中使王进卿至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370391_comment'></div>奉宣恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370391_comment'></div>赐臣前件僧尼告身并院额等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370391_comment'></div>臣伏以有为功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370391_comment'></div>莫大于化人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370391_comment'></div>无上菩提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370391_comment'></div>亦先于奉国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370391_comment'></div>臣以前因庆诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370391_comment'></div>辄贡敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370391_comment'></div>期降福于上天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370391_comment'></div>庶效祥于今古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370391_comment'></div>伏蒙陛下用至真之印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370391_comment'></div>转不退之轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370391_comment'></div>宠锡僧名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370391_comment'></div>荣颁院额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370391_comment'></div>仰窥金榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370391_comment'></div>跪捧瑶缄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370391_comment'></div>龙翥四维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370391_comment'></div>鸾回三点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370391_comment'></div>凭大悲之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370391_comment'></div>便至道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370391_comment'></div>承上圣之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370391_comment'></div>必成菩萨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370391_comment'></div>光生十地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370391_comment'></div>欢动一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370391_comment'></div>荷天眼之昭明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370391_comment'></div>愿法身之清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370391_comment'></div>所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370391_comment'></div>不获陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370391_comment'></div>无任欣戴之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1370391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　疑本年父承简卒，令狐楚解太原幕职，丁父忧。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='57b5d08e42294cdb80069a64e2bbacf3_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　令狐楚莅任前及任上，河东大旱，楚绥抚有方，境内晏然。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　李商隐应举未第，有上令狐楚状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　辟李商隐入幕。时赵皙或亦在令狐楚河东幕府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　二月后，在太原，有诗。作品：《游晋祠上李逢吉相公》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见于《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10738' /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　在河东节度使任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　早春，白居易、刘禹锡先后寄诗令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　白居易又寄《刘白唱和集》与楚，同时表示希望看到令狐楚与刘禹锡两人的唱和诗集。楚因致书禹锡，请编次两人唱和诗作。二月，刘将此前两人唱歌诗歌编成两卷，取名《彭阳唱和集》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　河东节度使任上，有文。作品：《盘鉴图铭记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四三。）</span><div id='poem_1370436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>盘鉴图铭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（833年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370436")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370436'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370436'>元和十三载二月八日。予为中书舍人翰林学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370436_comment'></div>夜直禁中。奏进旨检事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370436_comment'></div>因开前库东阁。于架上阅古今撰集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370436_comment'></div>凡数百家。偶于王勃集中卷末获此鉴图并序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370436_comment'></div>爱玩久之。翌日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370436_comment'></div>遂自摹写。贮于箱箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370436_comment'></div>宝历二年。乃命随军潘元敏绘于缣素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370436_comment'></div>传诸好事者。太原令狐楚记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370436_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1370436_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　楚始至太原任及罢任时，于灵石县有题石纪之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年6月</a>　六月，罢河东节度使，征拜吏部尚书，检校尚书左仆射。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　离太原前，令幕府从事李商隐代做书寄凤翔节度使李听。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永济（蒲州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='321620d1acb04f0f84b8cba40b16b4d3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("321620d1acb04f0f84b8cba40b16b4d3");'><span id='321620d1acb04f0f84b8cba40b16b4d3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=791&endYear=791')">791年</a>，26岁</div><div id='321620d1acb04f0f84b8cba40b16b4d3' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>及第后，与尹枢结伴归太原省亲，经河中，时卢纶在河中幕府，作诗送行。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在河中，作《登白楼赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（唐开元八年（公元720年），开蒲州为河中府，同年改为蒲州。乾元（公元758-760）时又改称河中府。以后历代屡有变动。《登白楼赋》今佚。）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
离石（石州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b80f4c645bb6478e8bead9f7b60dc4c6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b80f4c645bb6478e8bead9f7b60dc4c6");'><span id='b80f4c645bb6478e8bead9f7b60dc4c6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年</a>，27岁</div><div id='b80f4c645bb6478e8bead9f7b60dc4c6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年</a>　客石州，识刺史元韶。作品：《为石州刺史谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四〇。）</span><div id='poem_1370339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为石州刺史谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（792年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370339")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370339'>臣某言。伏奉某月日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370339_comment'></div>授臣石州刺史持节石州诸军事。谨以某月日到所部上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370339_comment'></div>祗奉明命。伏深战越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370339_comment'></div>臣某中谢。臣本琐材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370339_comment'></div>素无明略。虽被坚执锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370339_comment'></div>曾立丝发之功。而化人成俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370339_comment'></div>未知韦弦之政。岂意陛下录其微效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370339_comment'></div>委此无能。付臣以六条之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370339_comment'></div>委臣以千里之地。况离石古郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370339_comment'></div>洪河巨防。官惟其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370339_comment'></div>位不虚授。内顾庸劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370339_comment'></div>将焉克堪。誓当宣陛下之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370339_comment'></div>达其堙郁。布陛下之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370339_comment'></div>润其枯槁。少助神化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370339_comment'></div>微分圣忧。然后退居农亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370339_comment'></div>以避贤路。臣不胜悃款屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370339_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1370339_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
桂林（桂州）

id='poem_title_10729_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10729'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10729'>平日本多恨，新秋偏易悲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10729'>燕词如惜别，柳意已呈衰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10729'>事国终无补，还家未有期。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10729'>心中旧气味，苦校去年时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_10729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_10729'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_10729_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢敕书赐春衣并尺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（793年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370344")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370344'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370344_comment'></div>去二月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370344_comment'></div>中使某至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370344_comment'></div>伏奉敕书手诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370344_comment'></div>并赐臣春衣一副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370344_comment'></div>牙尺一条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370344_comment'></div>宸翰葳蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370344_comment'></div>宠锡稠謺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370344_comment'></div>捧受荣抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370344_comment'></div>如将不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370344_comment'></div>臣闻衣裳在笥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370344_comment'></div>与必有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370344_comment'></div>刀尺为器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370344_comment'></div>用惟其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370344_comment'></div>臣鲁国小儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370344_comment'></div>汉庭下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370344_comment'></div>因缘霈泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370344_comment'></div>污染官牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370344_comment'></div>颜尝忍愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370344_comment'></div>心不容忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370344_comment'></div>陛下仁发于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370344_comment'></div>惠周于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370344_comment'></div>矜臣以湿暑之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370344_comment'></div>赐之葛衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370344_comment'></div>念臣无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1370344", 1370344, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>忖度</span>之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370344_comment'></div>降其宝尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370344_comment'></div>轻新有楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370344_comment'></div>广狭不踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370344_comment'></div>被服而炎蒸坐销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370344_comment'></div>秉持而长短立辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370344_comment'></div>揆才量力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370344_comment'></div>将何补于分寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370344_comment'></div>运肘延颈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370344_comment'></div>实有尘于领袖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370344_comment'></div>当期毕命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370344_comment'></div>无以酬恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370344_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1370344_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为桂府王拱中丞贺南郊表</a><span class='authorDate'>（793年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370311")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370311'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370311'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370311_comment'></div>伏奉十一月十日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370311_comment'></div>南郊大礼毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370311_comment'></div>大赦天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370311_comment'></div>湛恩庞鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370311_comment'></div>大号涣汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370311_comment'></div>际天接地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370311_comment'></div>孰不庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370311_comment'></div>中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370311_comment'></div>臣闻禘尝之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370311_comment'></div>所以仁祖祢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370311_comment'></div>郊祀之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370311_comment'></div>所以尊天地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370311_comment'></div>五帝之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370311_comment'></div>蒉桴土鼓致其敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370311_comment'></div>敬有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370311_comment'></div>而礼不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370311_comment'></div>三王以降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370311_comment'></div>金罍玉斝备其礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370311_comment'></div>礼有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370311_comment'></div>而敬不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370311_comment'></div>秦之增封也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370311_comment'></div>觊望神仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370311_comment'></div>汉之郊丘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370311_comment'></div>禳除灾害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370311_comment'></div>虽无文而咸秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370311_comment'></div>终有废而莫举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370311_comment'></div>犹可以编在方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370311_comment'></div>垂其鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370311_comment'></div>岂若国家参文质于六经之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370311_comment'></div>陛下酌损益于百代之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370311_comment'></div>顺昊天之成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370311_comment'></div>得黎人之欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370311_comment'></div>九谷有年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370311_comment'></div>四方无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370311_comment'></div>然后因吉土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370311_comment'></div>迎长日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370311_comment'></div>咸池屡舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370311_comment'></div>太簇登歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370311_comment'></div>万灵识周旋之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370311_comment'></div>百神知飨献之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370311_comment'></div>云散而柴燎高达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370311_comment'></div>风清而萧芗远闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370311_comment'></div>信大报之无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370311_comment'></div>亦元鉴之不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370311_comment'></div>臣当时集军将官吏僧道百姓等丁宁宣示讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370311_comment'></div>惟天之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370311_comment'></div>莫遗于细微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370311_comment'></div>如日之辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370311_comment'></div>不隔于幽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370311_comment'></div>顽钝知感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370311_comment'></div>鬼神怀柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370311_comment'></div>何则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370311_comment'></div>刑莫大于成狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370311_comment'></div>陛下舍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370311_comment'></div>罪无轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370311_comment'></div>恩莫深于延赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370311_comment'></div>陛下推之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370311_comment'></div>泽及存殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370311_comment'></div>行道求志敢于直言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370311_comment'></div>既许以亲览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370311_comment'></div>触纶挂网屏于远方者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370311_comment'></div>又移之近郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370311_comment'></div>减来岁之新税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370311_comment'></div>昭其俭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1370311_comment'></div>弃比年之逋债。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1370311_comment'></div>宏诸仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1370311_comment'></div>念勋臣而树勋者益劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1370311_comment'></div>尊有德而不德者知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1370311_comment'></div>赐羸老有粟帛之优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1370311_comment'></div>礼神祇无牲币之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1370311_comment'></div>此所谓幽室尽晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1370311_comment'></div>枯条遍春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1370311_comment'></div>雷雨作而蛰虫昭苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1370311_comment'></div>风云行而笼鸟飞舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1370311_comment'></div>率土臣妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1370311_comment'></div>不胜大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1370311_comment'></div>况臣蒙被恩泽。<div id='poem_sentence_79_1370311_comment'></div>阻窥盛礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1370311_comment'></div>徘徊天外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1370311_comment'></div>目与心断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1370311_comment'></div>无任抃跃之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1370311_comment'></div>谨遣突将王清朝等奉表陈贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1370316_comment'></div>滂沱鸿恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370316_comment'></div>降自九天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370316_comment'></div>被于四海。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1370316_comment'></div>中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370316_comment'></div>臣闻天地之大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370316_comment'></div>本于生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370316_comment'></div>圣人之全功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370316_comment'></div>在乎化育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370316_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下至明立极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370316_comment'></div>大圣统天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370316_comment'></div>法贞观之宏规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370316_comment'></div>纂建中之盛业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370316_comment'></div>降哀矜于罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370316_comment'></div>一物不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370316_comment'></div>颁宠赠于忠勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370316_comment'></div>万方皆及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370316_comment'></div>事遵俭约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370316_comment'></div>道在宽宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370316_comment'></div>散作仁风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370316_comment'></div>洒为膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370316_comment'></div>率土臣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370316_comment'></div>不胜欢喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370316_comment'></div>臣限以监守。<div class='inline' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370399")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370399'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370399'>右。臣伏准贞元六年十一月八日敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370399_comment'></div>自今以后。诸州刺史县令以肆考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370399_comment'></div>如理术尤异。实效可称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370399_comment'></div>考满日委观察使录事迹以闻。特加奖擢者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370399_comment'></div>前件官守文惟谨。持法甚精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370399_comment'></div>清廉有馀。贞固无比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370399_comment'></div>臣伏见岭南。风俗惰懒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370399_comment'></div>苟避征徭。易成逋窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370399_comment'></div>张逊忧人若已。理郡如家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370399_comment'></div>劝课农桑。置立保社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370399_comment'></div>移风为敦厚之境。徵赋无惨急之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370399_comment'></div>周旋六年。其道一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370399_comment'></div>臣猥司廉察。忝守方隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370399_comment'></div>以所见闻。恳须甄录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370399_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1370399_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370337' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370337' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370337?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为道州许使君谢上表</a><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370337_comment'></div>如出井谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370337_comment'></div>而见日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370337_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370337_comment'></div>臣闻周室建侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370337_comment'></div>每先亲旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370337_comment'></div>汉朝置守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370337_comment'></div>必选循良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370337_comment'></div>臣公才蔑闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370337_comment'></div>利用无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370337_comment'></div>自幼及壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370337_comment'></div>终艰且拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370337_comment'></div>然而竭诚以许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370337_comment'></div>必尽力而在公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370337_comment'></div>一辞朝右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370337_comment'></div>累守郡佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370337_comment'></div>不寒自慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370337_comment'></div>无水而沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370337_comment'></div>伏惟陛下颁帝尧分命之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370337_comment'></div>敷孝宣共理之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370337_comment'></div>方须俊乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370337_comment'></div>以辑茕嫠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370337_comment'></div>若臣之伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370337_comment'></div>何敢望此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370337_comment'></div>不图恩从上降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370337_comment'></div>命自中出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370337_comment'></div>付以金印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370337_comment'></div>委之竹符。<div id='poem_sentence_33_1370337_comment'></div>荷天地之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370337_comment'></div>戴山为轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370337_comment'></div>感雨露之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370337_comment'></div>测海犹浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370337_comment'></div>谨以某月日便道到州上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370337_comment'></div>誓当佩韦以励志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370337_comment'></div>置水而清心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370337_comment'></div>酌远俗之便宜。<div id='poem_sentence_43_1370337_comment'></div>疲羸息肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370337_comment'></div>虽不足称陛下慎择眷求之意。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370337_comment'></div>不胜蹈舞天庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370337_comment'></div>无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1370337_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年</a>　在桂州王拱幕府。时父承简官太原府功曹参军，楚急于奉养，于年初解职离府，北归太原。作品：《谢敕书赐腊日口脂等表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span><div id='poem_1370349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢敕书赐腊日口脂等表</a><span class='authorDate'>（794年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370349")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370349'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370349'>臣某言。去年十二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370349_comment'></div>中使至。奉宣敕书手诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370349_comment'></div>兼赐臣口脂红雪各一合。十年历日一通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370349_comment'></div>捧缄跪发。以喜以骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370349_comment'></div>臣某中谢。臣闻平分四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370349_comment'></div>尧有历象。聚蓄百药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370349_comment'></div>周之宪章。至若雪散耀红紫之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370349_comment'></div>香膏蕴兰薰之气。合自金鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370349_comment'></div>贮以雕奁。是宜宠锡大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370349_comment'></div>荣加有德。用洒非常之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370349_comment'></div>式彰不次之恩。而臣远守岭隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370349_comment'></div>贱同凡器。曾无薄技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370349_comment'></div>上答殊私。陛下惠与露行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370349_comment'></div>德如天覆。发于中禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370349_comment'></div>及此下藩。谕以纶綍之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370349_comment'></div>颁其启闭之节。脂膏一润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370349_comment'></div>觉面目之有光。药石载攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370349_comment'></div>知肺腑之丢疾。誓当延年圣代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370349_comment'></div>戮力清朝。戴昊天而不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370349_comment'></div>瞻魏阙而增恋。无任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370349_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1370349_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
长治（潞州）

class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370336")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370336'>臣某言。中使第五守进至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370336_comment'></div>奉宣敕旨。擢臣知节度观察等留后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370336_comment'></div>臣即以今月十八日上讫。非常之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370336_comment'></div>降自宸衷。不次之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370336_comment'></div>猥加贱质。奉戴兢惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370336_comment'></div>罔知所图。臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370336_comment'></div>臣内顾孱庸。素无器业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370336_comment'></div>量力揣分。委质戎行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370336_comment'></div>身居将列。朝绝亲援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370336_comment'></div>不识公卿之第。粗闻宰辅之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370336_comment'></div>虽学孙吴。未知七德之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370336_comment'></div>尝师颜闵。不究六经之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370336_comment'></div>愚惟守直。讷未近仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370336_comment'></div>顾瞻等夷。每愧劣薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370336_comment'></div>苟求寡过之地。窃慕事君之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370336_comment'></div>刺发筮仕。逢盛时以自怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370336_comment'></div>执心许国。遇暗室而增惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370336_comment'></div>臣之愚素。敢忘恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370336_comment'></div>顷以陪臣。获随觐见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370336_comment'></div>比辞瑶陛。瞻睹天颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370336_comment'></div>遂因颁庆。窃膺宠锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370336_comment'></div>自谓生足荣矣。死无恨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370336_comment'></div>岂意圣慈焕发。睿奖曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370336_comment'></div>拔自辕门。寄之藩阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370336_comment'></div>洎天心特达。因屈朝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370336_comment'></div>而人望乖疏。必速官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370336_comment'></div>内念惶灼。浩无津涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370336_comment'></div>且上党重镇。赤狄遗人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370336_comment'></div>师旅荐兴。风俗难理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370336_comment'></div>猛则生怨。宽不知恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370336_comment'></div>邻接强暴。地当关塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370336_comment'></div>加之以仍岁灾沴。不足以两税徵科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370336_comment'></div>军政稍乖。压覆是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370336_comment'></div>臣虽竭股肱之力。沥肝胆之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370336_comment'></div>不知何以上答乾坤。少裨尘露云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370336_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1370336_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
华县（郑县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5d2f4b7d6bcb45efaef80a19fc098c17_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5d2f4b7d6bcb45efaef80a19fc098c17");'><span id='5d2f4b7d6bcb45efaef80a19fc098c17_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年</a>，53岁</div><div id='5d2f4b7d6bcb45efaef80a19fc098c17' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年4月</a>　四月，出为华州刺史，兼御史中丞，赐金紫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年</a>　秋，亲自主持华州乡试，革往年乡贡以权贵书信请托弊习，特试五场，卢弘止、马植先后就试，植以才取解元。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年</a>　李逢吉自剑南东川治所寄诗令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年11月</a>　十一月，河阳节度使乌重胤改横海节度使。皇甫镈擢楚为河阳怀节度使。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
沁阳（怀州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='75dd6954998b414d9f26dbbb2c1a20ff_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("75dd6954998b414d9f26dbbb2c1a20ff");'><span id='75dd6954998b414d9f26dbbb2c1a20ff_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=819')">818-819年</a>，53-54岁</div><div id='75dd6954998b414d9f26dbbb2c1a20ff' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年</a>　乌重胤率河阳兵士三千赴镇，士卒半道叛归，将为乱，适令狐楚赴河阳任，闻讯亲往慰抚，乱兵遂定。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年</a>　十二月十四日，到镇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年</a>　在河阳三城怀州节度使任上，有文。作品：《中书门下贺赦表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span>《送周先生住山记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四三。）</span>《河阳节度使谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span><div id='poem_1370317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书门下贺赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（818年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370317")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370317_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370317'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370317'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370317_comment'></div>伏见今日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370317_comment'></div>御丹凤门大赦天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370317_comment'></div>明照六幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370317_comment'></div>泽流九有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370317_comment'></div>臣等诚欢诚喜顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370317_comment'></div>臣闻覆帱生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370317_comment'></div>乾坤之盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370317_comment'></div>疆理化育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370317_comment'></div>帝王之极功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370317_comment'></div>伏惟睿圣文武皇帝陛下受天元符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370317_comment'></div>纂圣光宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370317_comment'></div>躬夏禹之勤俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370317_comment'></div>体帝尧之聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370317_comment'></div>除恶必绝其根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370317_comment'></div>耀武威而四凶既殛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370317_comment'></div>制政皆循其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370317_comment'></div>振文教而百度惟贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370317_comment'></div>今者东风发春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370317_comment'></div>元日献岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370317_comment'></div>凝旒视朝于正殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370317_comment'></div>步辇临御于应门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370317_comment'></div>开庞鸿之湛恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370317_comment'></div>孚涣汗之大号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370317_comment'></div>万物瞻睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370317_comment'></div>兆人允怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370317_comment'></div>至若移其放逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370317_comment'></div>解网之仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370317_comment'></div>吊彼伤残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370317_comment'></div>纳隍之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370317_comment'></div>罢开市之征税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370317_comment'></div>足以宏圣人厚下之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370317_comment'></div>褒卿士之祖先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370317_comment'></div>足以广圣人追远之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370317_comment'></div>潜蛰一振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370317_comment'></div>槁枯尽荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370317_comment'></div>普天率土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370317_comment'></div>不胜庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370317_comment'></div>臣某等谬司枢务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370317_comment'></div>虔奉德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370317_comment'></div>喜抃之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370317_comment'></div>倍百恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370317_comment'></div>无任庆跃屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1370317_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送周先生住山记</a><span class='authorDate'>（818年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370437")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370437'>先生姓周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370437_comment'></div>名隐遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370437_comment'></div>字息元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370437_comment'></div>宗其道者相号为太元先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370437_comment'></div>汝南人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370437_comment'></div>抱天和冲澹之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370437_comment'></div>含至精洁朗之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370437_comment'></div>玉冷泉润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370437_comment'></div>松高鹤闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370437_comment'></div>韬精守道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370437_comment'></div>冥得真契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370437_comment'></div>谷神既存而长守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370437_comment'></div>元关无键而不开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370437_comment'></div>贞元初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370437_comment'></div>游苏州吴县之包山林屋洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370437_comment'></div>秋八月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370437_comment'></div>始于洞西得神景观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370437_comment'></div>讯其居者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370437_comment'></div>曰距此数里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370437_comment'></div>世传毛公坞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370437_comment'></div>毛公道成罗浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370437_comment'></div>居山三百馀岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370437_comment'></div>有弟子七十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370437_comment'></div>聚石为坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370437_comment'></div>遗趾犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370437_comment'></div>尔能勤求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370437_comment'></div>吾请以导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370437_comment'></div>既行而萝筱迷密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370437_comment'></div>不知所往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370437_comment'></div>先生冥目久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370437_comment'></div>逢一物焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370437_comment'></div>双眸尽碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370437_comment'></div>毛色紫而本白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370437_comment'></div>高数尺馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370437_comment'></div>随而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370437_comment'></div>视乃鹿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370437_comment'></div>须臾乃跪止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370437_comment'></div>若有所告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370437_comment'></div>先生默记之而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370437_comment'></div>至十九年冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370437_comment'></div>刜木鬋茅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370437_comment'></div>奠厥攸居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370437_comment'></div>得异石一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370437_comment'></div>上有虫篆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370437_comment'></div>验之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370437_comment'></div>即毛公镇地符也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370437_comment'></div>既而凿户牖以为窦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370437_comment'></div>有鹤衔弄冠裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370437_comment'></div>戏舞于庭砌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370437_comment'></div>后得一井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370437_comment'></div>香白滑甘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370437_comment'></div>溢为白泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370437_comment'></div>其旁得古池焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370437_comment'></div>深广袤丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370437_comment'></div>阳验阴伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370437_comment'></div>湛如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370437_comment'></div>初先生尝息于洞之南门中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370437_comment'></div>神化恍惚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370437_comment'></div>往往失其所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370437_comment'></div>遇好风日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370437_comment'></div>亦来人閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370437_comment'></div>将至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370437_comment'></div>必先之以云鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370437_comment'></div>其弟子洒埽香室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370437_comment'></div>俄而至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1370437_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1370437_comment'></div>先生之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1370437_comment'></div>同乎无体矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1370437_comment'></div>不以昼夜更动息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1370437_comment'></div>不以寒暑易纤厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1370437_comment'></div>不食而甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1370437_comment'></div>走及奔马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1370437_comment'></div>全乎气者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1370437_comment'></div>虽饮而无漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1370437_comment'></div>止如灵龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1370437_comment'></div>外乎形者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1370437_comment'></div>鹿以导步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1370437_comment'></div>神柔异物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1370437_comment'></div>符以存视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1370437_comment'></div>道契先躅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1370437_comment'></div>井泉去厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1370437_comment'></div>昭乎仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1370437_comment'></div>池水不枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1370437_comment'></div>齐其虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1370437_comment'></div>仙云灵鹤之验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1370437_comment'></div>去来彷佛之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1370437_comment'></div>其必神行而智知乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1370437_comment'></div>予叔服膺先生之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1370437_comment'></div>二纪于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1370437_comment'></div>录先生本起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1370437_comment'></div>见命为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1370437_comment'></div>凝神遐想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1370437_comment'></div>直而不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1370437_comment'></div>元和十三年八月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1370437_comment'></div>华州刺史兼御史中丞令狐楚记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_94_1370437_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1370334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河阳节度使谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（818年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370334")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370334'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370334'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370334_comment'></div>伏奉前月二十七日诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370334_comment'></div>授臣朝议郎使持节怀州诸军事守怀州刺史御史大夫充河阳三城怀州节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370334_comment'></div>宠任非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370334_comment'></div>怔营失次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370334_comment'></div>巳再奉表陈谢讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370334_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370334_comment'></div>臣器质庸懦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370334_comment'></div>材能驽下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370334_comment'></div>文词小技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370334_comment'></div>不足饰身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370334_comment'></div>军旅大权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370334_comment'></div>未尝措意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370334_comment'></div>顷者叨居近密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370334_comment'></div>亲事圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370334_comment'></div>选擢皆出于宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370334_comment'></div>遭逢偶协于昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370334_comment'></div>进每忧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370334_comment'></div>退常乐天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370334_comment'></div>曾不知操舟者忌臣及津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370334_comment'></div>执辔者畏臣先路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370334_comment'></div>虽皎皎下烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370334_comment'></div>鉴一心之无瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370334_comment'></div>而营营谤兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370334_comment'></div>扇十手以相指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370334_comment'></div>去秋方半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370334_comment'></div>巳出严扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370334_comment'></div>今夏正中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370334_comment'></div>又离禁掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370334_comment'></div>伏惟睿圣文武皇帝陛下恩深君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370334_comment'></div>德厚乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370334_comment'></div>悯弃席之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370334_comment'></div>轸遗簪之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370334_comment'></div>微臣自临关辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370334_comment'></div>恭守章程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370334_comment'></div>非官办而政成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370334_comment'></div>幸人安而事集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370334_comment'></div>既无罪悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370334_comment'></div>亦望归还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370334_comment'></div>岂意便升疆场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370334_comment'></div>超授鈇钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370334_comment'></div>再麾飘飖而出守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370334_comment'></div>十乘隐辚以启行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370334_comment'></div>荷委寄而诚深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370334_comment'></div>苦离违之稍远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370334_comment'></div>就日积恋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370334_comment'></div>瞻天靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370334_comment'></div>拂儒冠以自惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370334_comment'></div>对朝服而增叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370334_comment'></div>以今月十四日到本镇上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370334_comment'></div>伏以郡称河内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370334_comment'></div>山倚太行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370334_comment'></div>古为雄藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370334_comment'></div>今号要地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370334_comment'></div>但缘疮痍未复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370334_comment'></div>杼轴巳空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370334_comment'></div>力欲辑绥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370334_comment'></div>曷由振举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370334_comment'></div>谨当拊循羸卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370334_comment'></div>字育疲氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370334_comment'></div>横征擅赋誓不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370334_comment'></div>峻法严科议不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370334_comment'></div>与之休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370334_comment'></div>使得便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370334_comment'></div>以此执心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1370334_comment'></div>期于报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1370334_comment'></div>前临河渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1370334_comment'></div>羡朝宗而指期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1370334_comment'></div>仰观众星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1370334_comment'></div>俟拱辰而何日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1370334_comment'></div>所守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1370334_comment'></div>不获诣阙辞让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1370334_comment'></div>无任感激攀恋涕咽之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1370334_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　在河阳节度使任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　在河阳任上，已赐紫金鱼袋。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　赴宣州，途径洛阳，与刘禹锡会面，时禹锡在洛阳丁母忧。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c4b66d9439094f7eae09aca987e50bba_label'><a href='javascript: /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=822&endYear=822')">822年10月</a>　闰十月，擢陕虢观察使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2011a47c01eb433f87443a927eb535ab_label'><a href='javascript: /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　在任上曾礼待陈商。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_10732'>丽藻飞来自相庭，五文相错八音清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10732'>初瞻绮色连霞色，又听金声继<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_10732'>才出山西文与武，欢从塞北弟兼兄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10732'>白头老尹三川上，双和<span class='link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年3月</a>　三月末，白居易罢刑部侍郎，以太子宾客分司东都。裴度、刘禹锡、张籍、韦行式等作诗送白居易，兼寄令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　白居易赴东都前有诗寄令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　在东都，与白居易往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　秋，白居易宿龙门，寄诗与楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　在东都留守任上，曾请刘禹锡撰家庙碑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　撰碑时，祖母柳氏已赠太原郡夫人，母孙氏累赠至魏国太夫人，父承简已累赠右仆射、太子太保。时弟令狐从检校膳部郎中从事河东幕府，弟令狐定已迁侍御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　在东都留守任上，姚合有诗寄令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　在东都留守任上，李商隐始受知于楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年11月</a>　十一月，检校右仆射兼御史大夫，充天平军节度使。<br /></div>

-----title
宣城（宣州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='47c0e0cd25ea491d9d1fa346ea1e0949_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("47c0e0cd25ea491d9d1fa346ea1e0949");'><span id='47c0e0cd25ea491d9d1fa346ea1e0949_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>，55岁</div><div id='47c0e0cd25ea491d9d1fa346ea1e0949' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　至宣州。时张祜自扬州往长安，途经宣州，令狐楚自草荐表，举祜入京。张祜至京后，因本年楚曾不愿荐元稹为知制诰，稹挟私怨，沮毁张祜，祜失意而归。作品：《进张祜诗册表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》五三九。）</span><div id='poem_1370324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进张祜诗册表</a><span class='authorDate'>（820年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370324")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370324_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370324'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370324'>凡制五言。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1370324", 1370324, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>苞含</span>六义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370324_comment'></div>近多放诞。靡有宗师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370324_comment'></div>前件人久在江湖。早工篇什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370324_comment'></div>研几甚苦。搜象颇深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370324_comment'></div>辈流所推。风格罕及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370324_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1370324_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年8月</a>　八月，甲申，楚任山陵使手下亲吏韦正牧、于翚以贪赃被决杖处死。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年8月</a>　己亥，令狐楚再贬衡州刺史，元稹草制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年9月</a>　九月，兵部员外郎李师素坐与令狐楚亲，贬资州刺史，再贬宾州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年9月15日</a>　九月十五日，令狐楚在宣州接到贬衡州刺史诏书。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙（潭州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1acfa3485b0542c8b9ef901531d71de0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1acfa3485b0542c8b9ef901531d71de0");'><span id='1acfa3485b0542c8b9ef901531d71de0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>，55岁</div><div id='1acfa3485b0542c8b9ef901531d71de0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　赴衡州，途径潭州时，寄诗李益。时益亦有诗寄楚。作品：《发潭州寄李宁常侍》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗》卷三三四。李益有诗《述怀寄衡州令狐相公》，见于《全唐诗》卷二八三。）</span><div id='poem_10728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>发潭州寄李宁常侍</a><span class='authorDate'>（820年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10728")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_10728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10728'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10728'>君今侍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_10728", 10728, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>紫垣</span>，我已堕青天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10728'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_10728", 10728, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>委废</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作弃）</span>从兹日，旋归在几年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10728'>心为西靡树，眼是北流泉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10728'>更过长沙去，江风满驿船。<div id='poem_sentence_3_10728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_10728'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_10728_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衡阳（衡州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a1a0a0f73e654cf8a3e5e561e8d3bee3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a1a0a0f73e654cf8a3e5e561e8d3bee3");'><span id='a1a0a0f73e654cf8a3e5e561e8d3bee3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=821')">820-821年</a>，55-56岁</div><div id='a1a0a0f73e654cf8a3e5e561e8d3bee3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年11月</a>　十一月，至衡州。有谢表。作品：《衡州刺史谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span><div id='poem_1370338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衡州刺史谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（820年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370338")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370338'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370338'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370338_comment'></div>去年九月十五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370338_comment'></div>于宣州伏奉某月日敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370338_comment'></div>贬授臣使持节衡州诸军事守衡州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370338_comment'></div>散官勋赐如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370338_comment'></div>仍驰驿发遣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370338_comment'></div>严威成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370338_comment'></div>忽降自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370338_comment'></div>战灼飞魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370338_comment'></div>如临于谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370338_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370338_comment'></div>臣素以凡品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370338_comment'></div>谬登高位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370338_comment'></div>虽满盈是戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370338_comment'></div>每刻肺腑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370338_comment'></div>而怨讟所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370338_comment'></div>难防颊舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370338_comment'></div>属奉陵无状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370338_comment'></div>选吏不精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370338_comment'></div>多偷见缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370338_comment'></div>连毙枯木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370338_comment'></div>擢臣之发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370338_comment'></div>岂可赎罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370338_comment'></div>粉臣之骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370338_comment'></div>不足胜刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370338_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下德厚于乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370338_comment'></div>明齐于日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370338_comment'></div>断自深虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370338_comment'></div>遽置宽科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370338_comment'></div>降受郡符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370338_comment'></div>锡留命服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370338_comment'></div>九重殊渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370338_comment'></div>再荷生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370338_comment'></div>万殒残骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370338_comment'></div>何由报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370338_comment'></div>以今月十二日到所部上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370338_comment'></div>伏以君亲同致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370338_comment'></div>臣子一例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370338_comment'></div>情有思于闻达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370338_comment'></div>理合具而奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370338_comment'></div>今臣官忝颁条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370338_comment'></div>职非奉使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370338_comment'></div>谢上之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1370338_comment'></div>拜章无因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1370338_comment'></div>欲隐默而不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1370338_comment'></div>惧中伤而未巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1370338_comment'></div>何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1370338_comment'></div>微臣顷蒙朝奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1370338_comment'></div>谬列宰司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1370338_comment'></div>诚不曾壅隔贤才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1370338_comment'></div>怨臣者至寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1370338_comment'></div>辞京之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1370338_comment'></div>毁臣者则多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1370338_comment'></div>今却望朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1370338_comment'></div>更无庇援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1370338_comment'></div>曲全孤贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1370338_comment'></div>唯托圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1370338_comment'></div>特乞眷慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1370338_comment'></div>俯鉴哀恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1370338_comment'></div>庶使穷鳞怀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1370338", 1370338, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>跃波</span>之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1370338_comment'></div>幽蛰有闻雷之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1370338_comment'></div>仰天垂涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1370338_comment'></div>伏地流汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1370338_comment'></div>不胜感恩惧罪战慄屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1370338_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1370338_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年4月</a>　四月，诏移郢州刺史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年5月14日</a>　夏至日，尚在衡州。作品：《夏至日衡阳郡斋书怀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10745' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10745' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10745?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏至日衡阳郡斋书怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（821年5月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10745")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_10745_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10745'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10745'>一来江城守，七见江月圆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10745'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_10745", 10745, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>齿发</span>将六十，乡关越三千。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10745'>褰帷罕游观，闭閤多沉眠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10745'>新节还复至，故交尽相捐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_10745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_10745'>何时羾阊阖，上诉高高天。<div id='poem_sentence_4_10745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_10745'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_10745_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
京山（郢州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7799b93a45204ef7a985ef7ab6fa6df2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7799b93a45204ef7a985ef7ab6fa6df2");'><span id='7799b93a45204ef7a985ef7ab6fa6df2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年</a>，56岁</div><div id='7799b93a45204ef7a985ef7ab6fa6df2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年</a>　发衡州，至郢州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年6月</a>　六月，河阳节度参谋兼监察御史韦珩揭发令狐楚等人任怀州刺史时因军需擅自额外加税一事，楚等各罚一月俸料。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年</a>　秋，曾寄诗江州刺史钱徽。作品：《秋怀寄钱侍郎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10734?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋怀寄钱侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（821年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10734")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_10734_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10734'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10734'>晚岁俱为郡，新秋各异乡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10734'>燕鸿一声叫，郢树尽青苍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10734'>山霞侵衣润，江风捲簟凉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10734'>相思如汉水，日夜向浔阳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_10734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_10734'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_10734_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3c0a89a39b4740d885fdf2904728c589_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3c0a89a39b4740d885fdf2904728c589");'><span id='3c0a89a39b4740d885fdf2904728c589_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年</a>，56岁</div><div id='3c0a89a39b4740d885fdf2904728c589' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年</a>　在郢州任上，与时任山南东道节度使的李逢吉唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年12月</a>　十二月，迁太子宾客，分司东都。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
武汉（鄂州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='afb16dd9b61b4b238b8a51be6a8f6d44_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("afb16dd9b61b4b238b8a51be6a8f6d44");'><span id='afb16dd9b61b4b238b8a51be6a8f6d44_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年</a>，56岁</div><div id='afb16dd9b61b4b238b8a51be6a8f6d44' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年</a>　冬、刘禹锡除夔州刺史，由洛阳赴任所，与令狐楚在鄂州相会。<br /></div>

-----title
襄阳（襄州）
-----detail

id='poem_10742' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10742' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10742?labeling=true' target='_blank'>将赴洛下旅次汉南献上相公二十兄言怀八韵</a><span
