-----title
三门峡（陕州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7719b580814a4fe5ac31b4e8fe5cfe2c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7719b580814a4fe5ac31b4e8fe5cfe2c");'><span id='7719b580814a4fe5ac31b4e8fe5cfe2c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=822&endYear=822')">822年</a>，57岁</div><div id='7719b580814a4fe5ac31b4e8fe5cfe2c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=822&endYear=822')">822年11月</a>　赴陕州，十一月上旬抵任，谏官上疏言不宜起用，视事一日，复改太子宾客，归东都。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封（汴州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2450adf301244875ae100a67f287b4d3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2450adf301244875ae100a67f287b4d3");'><span id='2450adf301244875ae100a67f287b4d3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=828')">824-828年</a>，59-63岁</div><div id='2450adf301244875ae100a67f287b4d3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年9月</a>　九月，迁宣武军节度使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　楚至任，锐意改革，去除弊政，以仁惠为治，汴州风俗为之一变。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　本年，令狐楚女已出嫁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　本年或明年，朱庆余游汴州，献诗令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　宣武军节度使任上，有文。作品：《贺南郊表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五三九。）</span><div id='poem_1370310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370310?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺南郊表</a><span class='authorDate'>（824年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370310")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370310'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370310'>臣某言。伏奉圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370310_comment'></div>以来年正月五日朝献太清宫飨太庙。七日有事于南郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370310_comment'></div>宜令所司准式者。敬莫大于朝宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370310_comment'></div>严莫大于飨郊丘。此二帝三王与圣祖神宗之所以总百灵而临万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370310_comment'></div>巍乎盛烈也。伏惟皇帝陛下光膺大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370310_comment'></div>茂对上元。尽诚信以奉先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370310_comment'></div>极婉愉而致养。孝光夷貊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370310_comment'></div>悌达神明。方将告成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370310_comment'></div>敷显号。惟天为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370310_comment'></div>俾众庶咸新。如日之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370310_comment'></div>与品物相见。六幽倾耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370310_comment'></div>四海翘首。凡在臣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370310_comment'></div>不胜庆幸。而臣谬贞师律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370310_comment'></div>叨守戎藩。不得捧豆笾于清庙之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370310_comment'></div>执玉帛于泰坛之下。仰观盛礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370310_comment'></div>伏贺鸿休。耸踊辕门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370310_comment'></div>无任恋结屏营之至。谨遣某官某奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370310_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1370310_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年</a>　在宣武节度使任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年3月</a>　三月，白居易由太子左庶子、分司东都除苏州刺史。二十九日，发东都。途径汴州，与令狐楚相聚五日而去。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年</a>　居易至苏州后，作诗记述汴州相会事，兼和令狐楚去年《到镇改月偶书所怀》诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年</a>　本年，汴州大治。刘禹锡在和州听说令狐楚政绩斐然，寄诗遥贺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年</a>　本年前后，改汴州郑州门为郑门，葺治郑门新亭，请刘禹锡作记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年</a>　本年或明年，曾寄诗白居易，诗在吴中一带广为流传。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=826&endYear=826')">826年</a>　在宣武节度使任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=826&endYear=826')">826年</a>　亳州传闻出圣水，饮者疾愈。令狐楚未加核实，以事奏上，受到宰相裴度判责。时浙西观察使李德裕亦上疏言其事妄，请加禁止。朝廷遂命令狐楚填塞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=826&endYear=826')">826年</a>　本年请随军潘元敏绘盘鉴图于绢素，传之好事者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=826&endYear=826')">826年</a>　本年前后，刘禹锡、王建、姚合分别寄诗令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=826&endYear=826')">826年</a>　宣武军节度使任上，有诗。作品：《奉送李相公重镇襄阳》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗续拾》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_28405' class='_poem'><div -----title
东平（郓州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ab3c086949fc47d9acd572b74b025208_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab3c086949fc47d9acd572b74b025208");'><span id='ab3c086949fc47d9acd572b74b025208_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　十一月，抵郓州任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　楚至郓州任清廉自守，克奉朝典。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　楚在郓州任辟韦正贯、李商隐入幕，韦充节度判官，李为巡官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　楚在郓州任。李商隐本为古文，在令狐楚幕府，楚工于今体章奏，因授其学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　弟令狐定本年或稍后迁职方员外郎，夜直曾有诗寄楚，姚合有和作。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=830&endYear=830')">830年</a>　在天平军节度使任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=830&endYear=830')">830年</a>　五月，奏改郓州东平县为天平县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=830&endYear=830')">830年</a>　武昌军使者至天平军，其副使窦巩请使者将自己与府主元稹的的唱酬之作示令狐楚，楚有酬和之作。作品：《和寄窦七中丞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见于《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10736?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鄂州使至窦七副使中丞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>见示与元<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>②</sup>相公献酬之什鄙人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>③</sup>任户部尚书时<span class='inlineComment2'>（《王》作「日」）</span>中丞是当司员外郎每示<span class='inlineComment2'>（《王》作「有」）</span>篇章多相唱和今因题四韵以寄所怀<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作和寄窦七中丞）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（829年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10736")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_10736_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_10736_0'>① 《王》作「窦巩中丞副使」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_10736_1'>② 《王》此下有「稹」字</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_10736_2'>③ 《王》作「余顷」</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10736'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10736'>仙吏秦城别，新诗鄂渚来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10736'>才推今八斗，职副旧三台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10736'>雕镂心偏许，缄封手自开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10736'>何年相赠答，却得在中台。<div id='poem_sentence_3_10736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_10736'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_10736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_10736'><span class='label'>按：</span>（录自《四部丛刊续编》影宋本《窦氏联珠集》，以王安石《唐百家诗选》〖简作《王》〗卷十四所录诗相校。（按：《全唐诗》卷三三四收此诗，题仅作《和寄窦七中丞》，诗中有误字，故重录之。同卷同人《秋怀寄钱侍郎》，《唐百寄诗选》作《郢城秋怀寄江州钱徽侍郎》，附记于此，以备徵考。）<br /></div><div id='poem_note_10736_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=830&endYear=830')">830年</a>　在郓州，楚于道场中识僧童蔡京，劝其还俗读书，与诸子同游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=830&endYear=830')">830年</a>　李商隐因府主令狐楚传授章奏之学，作诗致谢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=830&endYear=830')">830年</a>　李商隐在天平幕府与府主宴游唱和，备受恩遇。令狐楚岁给资装，令商隐赴京应进士试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年3月</a>　三月，衮海节度使庾承宣派副使李虞至天平节度治所，同天平建立良好关系。李虞事毕回府后，以故东平（郓州）太守苏源明《小洞庭五太守集序》、《秋夜小洞庭离宴序》二文寄与令狐楚，请楚立碑纪念。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年4月</a>　楚理郓有绩，四月，请刘禹锡作《天平节度使厅壁记》以记之。作品：《寄礼部刘郎中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗》卷三三四。刘禹锡作《酬令狐相公见寄》（《刘禹锡集》卷三三））</span><div id='poem_10723' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10723' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10723?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄礼部刘郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（831年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10723")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_10723_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10723'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10723'>一别三年在上京，仙垣终日选群英。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10723'>除书每下皆先看，唯有刘郎无姓名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10723'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_10723_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年7月</a>　七月，刻苏源明文上石，并撰文记之。刻碑时，已进爵彭阳县公。作品：《刻苏公太守二文记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四三。）</span><div id='poem_1370438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刻苏公太守二文记</a><span class='authorDate'>（831年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370438")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370438'>大和五年春三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370438_comment'></div>兖海节度副使李员外虞致本府书币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370438_comment'></div>修好于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370438_comment'></div>卒事返命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370438_comment'></div>且以故太守苏源明集中小洞庭宴籍及序二首见寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370438_comment'></div>请余立一贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370438_comment'></div>识其故处云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370438_comment'></div>余为之考寻图牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370438_comment'></div>询访耇老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370438_comment'></div>自五六日至于旬时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370438_comment'></div>茫然曾不得回源亭涡泊依稀彷佛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370438_comment'></div>从天宝十二载而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370438_comment'></div>及兹八十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370438_comment'></div>源明有盛名于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370438_comment'></div>遗爱在郓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370438_comment'></div>尝与五太守会集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370438_comment'></div>宴游之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370438_comment'></div>形于文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370438_comment'></div>囧若金玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370438_comment'></div>若良二千石好事君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370438_comment'></div>接武而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370438_comment'></div>纵不恢张增饰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370438_comment'></div>必当思人爱树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370438_comment'></div>存为此州故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370438_comment'></div>悲夫恩泽之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370438_comment'></div>四纪有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370438_comment'></div>自荡平而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370438_comment'></div>三政相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370438_comment'></div>不铦锋摩刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370438_comment'></div>以战斗为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370438_comment'></div>则长臂利爪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1370438_comment'></div>而攫拾是谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1370438_comment'></div>视嘉山水好风月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1370438_comment'></div>如越人之剃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1370438_comment'></div>瞽者之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1370438_comment'></div>非惟无用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1370438_comment'></div>又从而仇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1370438_comment'></div>余以为不可使中行子之文无传于此地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1370438_comment'></div>乃于溪亭作金石刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1370438_comment'></div>引而记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1370438_comment'></div>亦李志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1370438_comment'></div>秋七月二十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1370438_comment'></div>天平军节度等使检校尚书右仆射郓州刺史兼御史大夫彭城县公令狐楚记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1370438_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年10月</a>　十月，刘禹锡出为苏州刺史。冬，发长安，途经汴州时，令狐楚致信问候，并随信赠诗，禹锡作诗示谢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年11月</a>　十一月，朝廷命谏议大夫王彦威充勘定两税使，与天平节度使令狐楚等共同商定十二州应缴赋税。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年</a>　在天平任上，连年旱灾，楚均富济贫，民无流徙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　正月，在天平节度任上，有文。作品：《谢赐冬衣表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷五四○。）</span><div id='poem_1370348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370348'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370348'>臣某言。某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370348_comment'></div>中使至。伏奉敕书手诏等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370348_comment'></div>捧戴拜赐。荣感兢惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370348_comment'></div>军城欢抃。海曲光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370348_comment'></div>臣某中谢。伏惟尊号皇帝陛下至仁育物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370348_comment'></div>元德统乾。恩被生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370348_comment'></div>惠周遐迩。臣猥蒙寄任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370348_comment'></div>谬领方隅。寒暑骤移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370348_comment'></div>庶绩罔纪。王人忽降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370348_comment'></div>慈旨曲临。涉遐远之道途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370348_comment'></div>敷殊常之渥泽。诏书既启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370348_comment'></div>仰观垂露之华。珍服俯临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370348_comment'></div>实惧维鹈之刺。庆同戎府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370348_comment'></div>荣及闺门。况节戒元冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370348_comment'></div>恋深丹阙。授衣感自天之锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370348_comment'></div>尽力坚粉骨之诚。属垂溥天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370348_comment'></div>和布代化。万方昭泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370348_comment'></div>四海无虞。空知报效之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370348_comment'></div>愿同犬马。未展涓埃之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370348_comment'></div>何答邱山。寝兴靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370348_comment'></div>惭惧交集。无任受恩悃恳之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370348_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1370348_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　春，在天平节度任上，有诗。作品：《坐中闻思帝乡有感》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见于《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_10703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10703'>上酒忽闻吹此曲，坐中惆怅更何人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
汉中（褒城）
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　楚赴山南西道节度使任，中途取褒中路。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　楚抵山南西道节度治所兴元府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　时山南西道监军使为窦千乘。在兴元府，楚辟请赵柷、刘蕡、郑从谠、杜胜、李潘、李商隐等人入幕。其中赵柷为行军司马，郑从谠为节度使掌书记，杜胜为节度判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　李商隐或因应举，未远赴兴元幕，楚遂荐之于挚友刘禹锡，禹锡寄书愿招其入幕。商隐上状答谢楚举荐之恩，又有状答谢令狐楚赐绡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　本年秋，刘禹锡迁太子宾客分司东都，任上与令狐楚唱和颇多。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　本年，令狐楚将与李逢吉唱和诗歌编次成集，李逢吉旧时幕僚裴夷直为诗集取名《断金集》，并作序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　本年，令狐楚有诗悼李逢吉。作品：《李相薨后题<断金集>》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见于《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　本年或明年，白居易自洛阳寄诗令狐楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　春，楚有诗。作品：《春思寄梦得乐天》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见于《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span>《皇城中花园讥刘白赏春不及》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见于《全唐诗》卷三三四。）</span><div id='poem_10712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春思寄梦得乐天</a><span class='authorDate'>（836年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10712")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_10712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10712'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10712'>花满中庭酒满樽，平明独坐到黄昏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10712'>春来诗思偏何处，飞过函关入鼎门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10712'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_10712_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_10717' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10717' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10717?labeling=true' class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4572, "poem_allusion_10717")'>洛阳才子</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_10717_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10717'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10717'>五凤楼西花一园，低枝小树尽芳繁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10717'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4572, "poem_sentence_1_10717")'>洛阳才子</span>何曾爱，下马贪趋广运门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10717'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_10717_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　上年末或本年初，令狐绪兄弟至兴元省父，刘禹锡作诗相送。时绪已官国子博士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年2月</a>　二月，楚请刘禹锡作《山南西道节度使厅壁记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　李商隐因令狐父子荐引，进士及第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　李商隐登第后，上书令狐楚，感谢培养援引之恩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　夏初，李商隐自长安归济源省亲，离京前，致书于楚，约以中秋应兴元辟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　本年，令狐楚曾欲岁末告老致仕。夏，病，后病情转重。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　秋，楚有诗。作品：《九日黄白二菊花盛开对怀刘二十八》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见于《全唐诗续拾》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_10739' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_10739' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/10739?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九日黄白二菊花盛开对怀刘二十八</a><span class='authorDate'>（837年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_10739")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_10739_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_10739'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_10739'>西花虽未谢，二菊又初芳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_10739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_10739'>鬓云徒云白，腰金未是黄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_10739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_10739'>曙花淩露彩，宵艳射星芒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_10739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_10739'>日正开边树，风清发更香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_10739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_10739'>山椒应散乱，篱下倍荧煌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_10739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_10739'>泛酒遥相忆，何由共醉狂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_10739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_10739'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_10739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_10739'><span class='label'>（见蒲积中《古今岁时杂咏》卷三五）（按：</span>此诗原署「相公」，其次为刘禹锡和诗「素萼迎寒秀」云云，检刘诗收《刘宾客外集》卷四，题作《和令狐相公九日对黄白二菊花见怀》，知此诗为楚作。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_10739_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　李商隐闻楚病，驰赴兴元幕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年9月</a>　九月贾岛坐飞谤，得令狐楚之助，责授遂州长江县主簿。贾岛赴任途中，寄诗令狐楚。到任后，楚寄赠寒衣，岛复以诗答谢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　冬，楚以病重，上表请求解职，赴京就医。或因上表后病情危笃，未成行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　楚病重时，子令狐绪、令狐绹、令狐纶兄弟至兴元侍父。时绹已迁左补阙，纶官左武卫兵曹参军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　楚卒前五日，有诗书寄刘禹锡。已佚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　楚卒前四日，召诸子，命之后事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　楚卒前三日，尚吟咏赋诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　楚卒前一日，召从事李商隐助草遗表，劝谏文宗对大和九年夏秋牛李两党贬谴者及甘露事变受害者或降恩或昭雪。又叮嘱诸子在己死后勿请谥号，丧事从简。作品：《遗疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见于《全唐文》卷五四一。）</span><div id='poem_1370358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1370358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1370358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>遗疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（837年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14025, "中唐", "令狐楚", "poem_title_1370358")'>令狐楚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1370358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1370358'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1370358'>臣永惟际会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1370358_comment'></div>受国深恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1370358_comment'></div>以祖以父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1370358_comment'></div>皆蒙褒赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1370358_comment'></div>有弟有子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1370358_comment'></div>并列班行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1370358_comment'></div>全要领以从先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1370358_comment'></div>委体魄而事先帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1370358_comment'></div>此不自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1370358_comment'></div>诚为甚愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1370358_comment'></div>但以永去泉扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1370358_comment'></div>长辞云陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1370358_comment'></div>更陈尸谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1370358_comment'></div>犹进瞽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1370358_comment'></div>虽号叫而不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1370358_comment'></div>岂诚明之敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1370358_comment'></div>今陛下春秋鼎盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1370358_comment'></div>寰海镜清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1370358_comment'></div>是修教化之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1370358_comment'></div>当复理平之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1370358_comment'></div>然自前年夏秋已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1370358_comment'></div>贬谴者至多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1370358_comment'></div>诛戮者不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1370358_comment'></div>伏望普加鸿造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1370358_comment'></div>稍霁皇威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1370358_comment'></div>殁者昭洗以云雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1370358_comment'></div>存者沾濡以雨露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1370358_comment'></div>使五谷嘉熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1370358_comment'></div>兆人安康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1370358_comment'></div>纳臣将尽之苦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1370358_comment'></div>慰臣永蛰之幽魄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1370358_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年11月12日</a>　十一月十二日，卒于兴元官舍。<br /></div>
